> "Ivyo bimeze gute ku buhinga butera ingorane? Bitcoin ni umuguzi-atazwi, umuguzi-atazwi cryptocurrency ata banki nkuru, kandi ata mahera yo gucuruza. Ukoresheje iciyumviro gisa na Hashcash, abaguzi baturira CPU cycles bagerageza kuvumbura bimwe mu 21,000 eventually isoko ko It bizoba e,000 igihe. ya Bitcoins izoshika ku rugero rumwe n'inguvu zikenewe kugira ngo zibe generate, bizovamwo amafaranga ashigikiwe n'inguvu atashobora gushika kuri Leta iyo ari yo yose."

Abagize ihuriro benshi baratanga ivyiyumviro vyo kunoza iki canditswe. Satoshi [arabigiramwo uruhara] we ubwiwe amasaha makeyi inyuma y’ubutumwa bwa mbere kugira ngo atange iciyumviro ciwe. Yandika ko "ashima vy'ukuri utwigoro," ariko ko "hari ingorane nyinshi", hanyuma akavuga urutonde rwa Elements zimubabaza:



- Ku bijanye n’ukutagira akosho ka Leta, aragira ubwenge mu kwandika ko «ata nkeka ko yinjira muri ubwo bwoko bw’ugutera ubwoba canke kwirega»; (*original: "'Abateguye biteze ko ivyo bizovamwo amafaranga ahagaze-ku-vyerekeye-inguvu atashobora gushikwako na Leta iyo ari yo yose.' – Nta gukeka ko ntaco ndiko ndatwenga canke ngo ndiko ndavuga."*)
- Ku bijanye n'ugushigikirwa n'inguvu, abona ko amafaranga "atashikamye ku bijanye n'inguvu" yongerako ati: "Iki kibazo caravuzweko. Ntigifitaniye isano n'igiciro c'inguvu. Igitigiri ca NLS gishingiye ku nguvu cari intango nziza, ariko inguvu z'isoko zizorushiriza kuganza.";
- Ku bijanye n'umuce w'ivyo bikoresho bitamenyekana, avuga ko adashaka "gushira ahabona umuce w'ivyo 'bimenyekana'" kandi ko yari "yafise umugambi wo guhindura urubuga rw'intango" muri ivyo. (*original "Ntidushaka kurongora 'atazwi'. (Nari mfise insiguro yo guhindura urubuga rw'intango)"*)


Mu [ikete] (https://mmalmi.github.io/Satoshi/#email-197) ryandikiwe Martti Malmi amasaha makeyi aheze, Satoshi itanga imvo zibiri nyamukuru zo gusigura iyo ntumbero yo gufata minenerwe ukutamenyekana: akaga ku wukoresha n’ukuntu abantu bose babibona. Yandika ati:


> "Ngira ngo dukwiye gukuraho ugushimika ku bijanye n'ukutamenyekana. Kubera ko amaderesi ya Bitcoin azwi cane aho kohereza kuri IP, ntidushobora gutanga iciyumviro c'uko vyose bihita bimenyekana. Birashoboka ko umuntu aba uwutamenyekana, ariko utegerezwa kwiyubara. kuvyerekeye ataco tubiteza imbere."

Asozera ubutumwa bwiwe kuri iyo nama ati:


> "Mbabarira kuba ndi uburengeti butose. Kwandika insobanuro y'iki kintu ku bantu bose ni Hard. Ntaco cobifatanya."

Mu nyuma, Teppy yarahinduye iyo nsiguro, azirikana ivyiyumviro vyari vyatanzwe. Gutyo, mu ntango z’ukwezi kwa Mukakaro, vyabonetse ko insiguro yari ikikuje Bitcoin yari itunganijwe neza, ivyo bikaba vyerekana ko yari yiteguye kugira ngo abantu benshi baze baze mu buryo butagira uko bungana.


### Ivyacitse!


Ku wa 11 Nyakanga 2010, harasohotse igitabu casubiwemwo c’ikiganiro ca Bitcoin canditswe na Teppy ku wa S. Yari isomwa gutya:


> "Ivyo bimeze gute ku buhinga butera ingorane? Bitcoin ni amafaranga y'urunganwe, ashingiye ku rubuga ata banki nkuru, kandi ata mahera yo gukoresha. Ukoresheje iciyumviro ca Proof-of-Work, ama node aturira inzinguzingu za CPU arondera imigwi y'ibiceri, atangaza ivyo yabonye ku isoko ry'urubuga. hejuru y'agaciro k'inguvu zikenewe kugira ngo zibe generate, bikaba vyerekana ko abarundi barizigiye ko ayo mafaranga azoguma hanze y'ubushobozi bwa Leta iyo ari yo yose."

![Slashdot Logo in 2010](assets/en/043.webp)


Ico gitabu carabonywe, kandi abantu hafi 500 barashizeko amajambo mu misi mikeyi. Ku bwa Bitcoin, ivyo vyatumye abantu benshi cane baza kuri uwo muhora no ku nama. Ikoreshwa rya Blockchain ryarateye imbere cane: igitigiri c’ibikorwa vyakozwe kuri iyo nzira caraduze kiva kuri 42 ku wa 10 Nyakanga kija ku 1.641 ku wa 12, kigera ku 5.554 ku wa 14, kikaba ari igitigiri kinini kuruta ibindi vyose. Uwo murongo waragumyeho naho umuzigo wariko uragwira. Ku wa 14, umuhinga mu bijanye n’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none Gavin Andresen [yanditse] ku rubuga rw’ihuriro:


> "Ngira ngo Satoshi yakoze igikorwa ciza cane: mu misi ibiri iheze igihe Bitcoin yari 'slashdotted', sinari numvise ingorane iyo ari yo yose y'ugutakaza amafaranga y'ubudandaji bwa Bitcoin, canke igihe c'uguhagarara kw'urubuga kubera umuzigo, canke ingorane iyo ari yo yose yerekeye imikorere y'ishimikiro.

Inkurikizi ya mbere y’ivyo bitero ni uko igiciro ca Bitcoin caduze cane, kiva ku madolari 0,008 kija ku madolari 0,08 mu ndwi imwe, ivyo bikaba ari ukuduga incuro cumi!


Iyindi ngaruka y’ukwinjira kw’abantu bava kuri Slashdot ni ububasha bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none bukoreshwa kuri iyo nzira. Abantu benshi batangura iyo porogarama bagakora ama blocs bakoresheje processeurs zabo zo hagati. Hagati y’italiki 11 n’italiki 17 Nyakanga, igipimo ca Hash caraduze kiva kuri 0,22 GH/s kija kuri 2,78 GH/s.


### Ivyaremwe vy'umusozi Gox


Mu bavumbuye Bitcoin kubera Slashdot harimwo Jed McCaleb, umunyamerika w’imyaka 35, akaba n’umuhinga mu vy’ubuhinga bwo gukora porogarama, azwi cane mu gushinga no gutegura porogarama yo gusangira amadosiye n’abandi yitwa eDonkey2000 mu myaka ya 2000. Kubera ko yabonye ingorane zo kuronka Bitcoin muri Exchange ku madolari, yaciye afata ingingo "ku ntumbero" yo guhingura isoko ryiza. Kugira ngo abikore, yasubiyemwo umwe mu migambi yiwe ya kera yateguye mu 2007: Ubupfumu bw’Ikoraniro ryo kuri Internet Exchange (MTGOX), urubuga rwari rwemereye kugura no kugurisha amakarata y’urukino rwo kuri Internet *Ubupfumu: Ikoraniro ryo kuri Internet*. Yasubiye gukoresha izina ry'urubuga rw'uwo mugambi (mtgox.com), ryacitse izina ry'urubuga rushasha: Mt. Gox, rivugwa ngo "Mount Gox".


![Jed McCaleb in 2013](assets/en/044.webp)

Jed McCaleb mu 2013 (inkomoko: Ariel Zambelich ku rubuga rwa [Wired]))


Haciye indwi imwe, ku wa 18 Nyakanga, Jed McCaleb yaratanguje urubuga rwiwe rwa Exchange maze [aratangaza] ku rubuga rw’ihuriro. Kubera ubuhinga bwiwe, yaratumye iyo nzira ikora nk’isoko ry’ubuhinga bwa none, nk’uko bimeze mu guhanahana amakuru kuri Internet muri iki gihe. [Nk'uko yabivuze], yari itandukanye n'isoko rya Bitcoin kubera ko "yama iri kuri interineti, yikora," "urubuga rwari rwihuta kandi rwari rufise ubucuti bwihariye," kandi "Interface yari nziza cane." Ivyo vyatumye Mt. Gox yihuta kuba uburyo nyamukuru bwo kuronka Bitcoin, yishingira intahe nk’ikigereranyo c’ugutanga amadolari.


![Interface of the Mt. Gox platform in February 2011](assets/en/045.webp)

Interface y’urubuga rwa Mt. Gox muri Ruhuhuma 2011 (inkomoko: [ububiko bwa Mt. Gox]


Mu ntango, iyo nzira yemera kwishura biciye kuri PayPal. Ariko rero, mu kwezi kwa Gitugutu 2010, inyuma y’aho abantu benshi cane basavye ko bamusubiza amahera, PayPal yarabujije konti ya Jed McCaleb, ivyo bikaba vyatumye ahagarika amahera yashize kuri iyo nzira no kuyakuramwo amahera mu gihe gito. Haciye indwi nkeyi, [yaragaruye] amahera yoherezwa mu kwongerako Liberty Reserve nk’uburyo bwo kwishura. Hanyuma, yaremera kandi amahera yoherezwa biciye kuri [Paxum](Paxum](https. amadolari] (ACH) na [mu mayero] (insiguro=2515.msg34040#0)PA340).


### Ingaruka zituma Slashdotting yihuta


Ingaruka zo gusohora intangamarara ya Bitcoin kuri Slashdot zari zitangaje ku mugambi wa Satoshi Nakamoto. Ukwiyongera kw’abantu bashimishijwe kwatumye igiciro kigira agaciro kanini cane kandi n’igipimo ca Hash kiduga. Ikindi kandi, vyatumye umuntu umwe yitwa Jed McCaleb abona Bitcoin maze ashiraho isoko rikwiye ryo gucururizamwo igice c’ibarabara citwa Mt. Gox.

Mu mezi yakurikiye, ubuhinga, ubutunzi, n’iterambere rya Mining vyarateye imbere cane, bituma Slashdot iba intango nyayo ya Bitcoin nk’umuhari w’abanyagihugu. Ariko rero, amahinduka akomeye cane yabaye ku rwego rwa porogarama n’urw’amaporotokole: ubugoyagoye bukomeye bwari bukwiye gukosorwa. Ikigabane gikurikira kivuga cane kuri ivyo bibazo vy’ubuhinga, bikaba ari intambwe ihambaye mu gutegura Bitcoin.


## Ibibazo vya mbere vy'ubuhinga

<chapterId>30cc4fe4-22b0-429e-9874-029c9137c0aa</chapterId>


Nk’uko vyavuzwe mu kigabane ca nyuma, uruja n’uruza rw’abakoresha bavuye kuri Slashdot ku wa 11 Nyakanga 2010, rwatumye abantu benshi bakunda umugambi wa Satoshi Nakamoto. Ikoreshwa ry’iyo nzira ryarateye imbere cane, kandi igipimo ca Exchange caraduze incuro cumi, nk’uko nyene ububasha bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none bwari bugenewe iyo nzira. Gutyo, Bitcoin yarateye imbere cane mu ci.


Ariko rero, ivyo vyari biherekejwe n’ibibazo vy’ubuhinga, aho habonetse utunenge tumwetumwe muri iyo porogarama. Kumenyekana cane vyasobanura ko abantu benshi basuzuma iyo kode kandi ko hariho n’ibishoboka vyinshi bitari vyo mu bikorwa. Kandi ivyo ni vyo nyene vyabaye ku wa 15 Myandagaro n'ivyabaye vy'ugusesagura agaciro, "ugusenyuka" kwa mbere mu mateka ya Bitcoin, kwamaze nk'amasaha 15. Ico kiringo cararanzwe n’iterambere ry’ubuhinga bwa none, kugira ngo umuntu abone imbere y’igihe ibintu bitandukanye bishobora kumutera ubwoba no gukosora amakosa uko bishoboka kwose.


### Kunoza porogaramu


Ukwiyongera kw’abakoresha Slashdot na kwo nyene kwatumye bikenerwa ko iyo porogarama itera imbere. Ivyiyumviro bitari vyo vyabonetse vyari bikwiye gukosorwa, kandi hariho ibintu bishasha vyari bikwiye gushirwamwo. Satoshi rero yari mu ngorane: ku wa 18 Nyakanga, yarabwiye Martti Malmi mu mwiherero ko "yariko aratakaza ubwenge bwanje ko hari vyinshi bikwiye gukorwa." Mu mezi abiri, harasohotse amaverisiyo makeyi atari munsi y’umunani y’iyo porogarama!

Ariko rero, uwaremye Bitcoin ntariko arakora kuri kode gusa. Ashobora kwizigira Gavin Andresen, yashitse muri Ruheshi kandi ariko ararushiriza kwitabira iterambere (arafise icubahiro ku bubiko bwa SourceForge kuva ku wa 9 Nyakanga). Abantu bamwebamwe barashaka kumenya ingene iyo nzira ikora, bagaca bamenyesha ibibazo iyo bahuye navyo, nka Christian Decker (cdecker) canke Michael Marquardt (azwi cane kw’izina ry’uruyeri rya Theymos). Satoshi kandi ishigikirwa n’abacukuzi, bahindura kode kugira ngo barondere uburyo bwo gutuma ibice bimera neza, nka ArtForz (umuntu wa mbere yashinze itongo rya Mining, nk’uko tuzobibona mu kigabane gikurikira), umuhinga mu vy’ubuhinga bw’amabuye y’agaciro w’Umudagi Nils Schneider (tcatm), Michael Brown (knightmb), canke BlackEye.


Ubwa nyuma, turashobora kuvuga Jeff Garzik (akoresheje izina ry’uruyeri jgarzik ku rubuga), umunyamerika w’umuhinga mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwa none kandi atanga umusanzu mw’isi y’ubuhinga bwa none, cane cane mu bijanye n’ugukwiragiza Red Hat, akaba n’umuyoboke w’ishure ry’ubutunzi ryo muri Otirishiya. Yavumbuye Bitcoin biciye mu kiganiro co kuri Slashdot maze hafi ubwo nyene aca yinjira muri Bitcoin.


![Jeff Garzik in 2013](assets/en/046.webp)

Jeff Garzik mu 2013 (isoko: [Benson Samweli] (kuvugana-na-Jeff-garzik/))


Intumbero ya mbere ya Satoshi ni ugutuma porogarama n’imirongo ngenderwako biguma bitekanye, kugira ngo bishobore guhangana n’ukwiyongera kw’ikoreshwa ryavyo vuba. Bafatanije na Gavin Andresen, barihweza ibitero bitandukanye bishobora gushika (harimwo n’ibitero vyo kwanka gukora) maze bagaharanira gukosora utunenge twavumbuwe. Uko ni ko urutonde rw’ibibanza vyo gusuzuma rwongerwa ku wa 17 Nyakanga ([v0.3.2](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=437.msg3807#msg3807)), bikabuza uruzitiro gusubira kwandikwa imbere y’itariki kanaka y’igikorwa, kandi iciyumviro co ku wa 5 Nyakanga. ([v0.3.3]([v0.3.3])) kugira ngo utunganye uburyo bwo guhitamwo uruhererekane rwiza n’ibihimba.


Gavin na Satoshi na bo nyene barakosoye ibibazo vyinshi. Igihambaye muri ivyo ni "1 RETURN bug," ubugoyagoye buri muri sisitemu y'inyandiko bwatumye bishoboka gukoresha amafaranga y'ama bitcoins avuye kuri Address iyo ari yo yose akoresheje inyandiko yihariye. ArtForz yatangaje iyo nzira y’ubugoyagoye ku wa 28 Nyakanga, aho gukoresha iyo nzira y’ubugoyagoye no kwitunga mu buryo bw’ubukerebutsi, yahisemwo gusangira ivyo yavumbuye na Satoshi na Gavin. Satoshi yaciye yihuta gushiramwo ivyo gukosora muri porogarama ([v0.3.6] ([v0.3.6]) maze asaba ko abakoresha bose basubiramwo. Gutyo, Bitcoin yararokotse ibintu vyari gushobora gutuma igira ingorane. MITRE yaje kwandika iyo nzira y’ubugoyagoye munsi y’ikimenyetso [CVE-2010-5141](CVE-2010-5141).


Intumbero ya kabiri yari iyo gutuma iyo porogarama ikora neza mu guhindura ingene iyo porogarama ikora canke mu gutuma iyo porogarama ikora neza. Ni muri iki kiciro aho kwongerako amakode y'imikorere ya `OP_NOP` ku rutonde rw'inyandiko rw'imbere bigwa, vyakozwe mu buryo bw'ubute na Satoshi ku wa 29 Nyakanga (v0.3.6), n'ivyo [ibivugwa] vyonyene. Izo kode z'ibikorwa ni amabwirizwa ataco akora iyo ari mu nyandiko, ariko ntizihindura ubusa igikorwa. Ku bw’ivyo, umuntu arashobora guhindura inyifato y’ayo mabwirizwa ataco atuma inyandiko zidahuye n’iyindi verisiyo ya kera y’amaporotokole, ni co gituma Satoshi yavuze ivyo. Izo kode z'ibikorwa zoshobora kwemera cane cane ivyo vyokwitwa "amaforogo ya Soft" mu 2015 na 2016, mu guhindura amabwirizwa `OP_NOP2` na `OP_NOP3` mu `OP_CHECKLOCKTIMEVERIFY` na `OP_CHECKSIQUENCE`Ivyitezwe).


Abacukuzi na bo nyene barasangira ivyo bavumbuye kugira ngo batere imbere, mu buryo butaziguye canke butaziguye, uruvyaro rwa bitcoins n’ubuhinga nyamukuru. Ica mbere, [ugutuma Laszlo akora neza] (ivyo Laszlo yakoze] vyashizwe muri porogarama ku wa 6 Nyakanga (v0.3.0). Hanyuma, [ububiko bw’ibintu] (ububiko bw’ibintu] (insiguro=501.msg5815#msg5815) bw’igikorwa ca SHA-256 Hash cakozwe na Nils Schneider be n’[ugutuma n’ivyo BlackEye yongereye kuri iyo porogarama ku wa 29 Nyakanga (v0.3.6). Ubwa nyuma, [uguhuza ibiharuro ku gikoresho kimwe](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=648.msg6722#msg6722) vyashikirijwe na Nils Schneider (na none) vyari [vyuzuye] mu gitabu c’amategeko ku wa 15 Myandagaro (v0.3.10).


Ivyo vyose bitera imbere bisigura ko Bitcoin iriko irakomera uko bukeye uko bwije mu bijanye n’ugukora kwa porogarama n’ugukora kwa Mining. Ariko rero, ikintu gitera ikimenyetso cane mu kibano kirahumanya mu buryo bumwe iyo nzira y’ubuhinga bushasha. Ico kintu c’ugusesagura agaciro cabaye muri Myandagaro, gica gihungabanya urubuga amasaha nk’icumi n’atanu.


### Ivyabaye vy'agaciro karengeye


Ku wa 15 Myandagaro 2010, nk'isaha zitanu z'ijoro (UTC), igice kirimwo amafaranga yatumye habaho amafaranga arenga 184 *miliyaridi* z'ama bitcoins congerewe ku ruzitiro ku burebure bwa 74.638. Ivyo bimenyetso vy’agaciro kanini cane vyakoresheje ubugoyagoye bwo kwibuka mu guserukira ibiharuro: uwutera yararemye ibisohoka bibiri vy’ugucuruza vy’ibiharuro 92.233.720.368.54277039 BTC kimwe cose, igiharuro kiri hafi y’ibiharuro vy’agaciro kuruta ibindi vyose bishobora guserukirwa n’umubare w’ibiharuro (64-).


Haciye isaha imwe, ingorane yabonywe na Jeff Garzik, uwagabishije abarundi bose ku bijanye n'"ikintu kidasanzwe". Inyishu ya Satoshi yaje nk’isaha icenda z’ijoro: [yasohoye] ihinduka ry’intango ry’itegeko ku nama n’ [yahanuriye] abantu "guhagarika gutanga". Amaze gusubiramwo ibintu bimwebimwe no kubishira kuri Sourceforge, amaherezo [arasohora] igikoresho co gukoresha Windows, Linux, na Mac OS X ku isaha ya 23:48 z’ijoro.


Ico gipande caratuma abacukuzi banka iyo nzira y’ubudandaji nk’iyitagira akamaro, bagashiraho irindi shami ritagiramwo iyo nzira. Igipande ca mbere c’iri shami cabonetse isaha 23:53 z’ijoro.


Bukeye mu gitondo, haciye igihe gitoyi isaha umunani z’ijoro, iyo ntambara yarakemutse. Uruzitiro rwiza rwacitse rurerure kuruta urundi, ivyo bikaba vyasobanura ko utugingo ngengabuzima twose twategerezwa gukurikira urwo ruzitiro, yaba yashizeko igipande canke atari co. Ivyo vyatumye ibikorwa vy’urubuga bihungabana mu kiringo c’amasaha nka 15, ariko ukuntu abanyabubasha bavyakiriye vyari akarorero. Satoshi [yanditse] (insiguro=823.ubutumwa9734#ubutumwa9734) nk'isaha imwe y'ijoro:


> "Bisa n'uko twarengeye uruzitiro rubi ahantu hafi 74689. &nbsp;0.3.9 n'ibindi bihimba vyo hasi vyamaze amasaha bishura n'umubare w'ibarabara ry'ubu. (...) Turashimira bose ku kwishura vyihuse!"

### Uburyo bwo kugabisha

Amaze kuvumbura ikibazo ca 1 RETURN muri Nyakanga, Satoshi Nakamoto yarakoze ibishoboka vyose kugira ngo akingire urubuga impanuka. Ku wa 3 Myandagaro, yongeyeko uburyo bwo kugabisha kuri porogarama ikora iyo uruzitiro rwacitsemwo ibice ([v0.3.8] Ariko rero, ubwo buryo bwagaragaye ko butagira akamaro mu kumenya ikibazo c’ugusesagura agaciro cavutse ku wa 15, bituma Satoshi yihutisha [umugambi wiwe] (https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=823.msg9586#msg9586) kugira ngo akore uburyo buteye imbere kuruta.


Mu misi yakurikiye ivyo bintu, Satoshi rero yubatse uburyo bwiza bwo kugabisha ku rubuga, ivyo bikaba vyamufashije, afise urufunguzo rw’ibanga, kugabisha ama node iyo habaye ingorane z’ubuhinga no guhagarika amabwirizwa amwamwe ya API. Ku wa 22 Myandagaro, [yashize ahabona] ubuhinga bwiwe ku rubuga rw’ihuriro. Iryo tangazo ryatumye abanywanyi bagira amaganya, babonye ko muri iyo nzira hari ikintu co gushiramwo ibintu vyose hamwe n’ubugoyagoye Leta ishobora gukoresha. Satoshi [yasubije] (yasubije] (https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=898.msg11074#msg11074) haciye imisi ibiri, yita ivyo vyiyumviro "paranoid" kandi asobanura ko iyo sisitemu ishobora guhagarara n'amaboko n'abakoresha kandi ko yoba ari ivy'akanya gatoyi uko biri kwose.


Ku wa 27 Myandagaro, uburyo bwo kugabisha bwashizwe muri porogarama ([v0.3.11] ([v0.3.11])). Ivyo guhagarika ibikorwa vyari [vyakuweho] (insiguro=2228.msg29479#msg29479) mu kwezi kwa kigarama. Mu myaka yakurikiye, iyo nzira yo kugabisha yarakoreshejwe incuro nyinshi, cane cane ku mpanuka Fork mu 2013, imbere y’uko [ikurwaho] burundu (https://Bitcoin.org/alert/2016-11-01-alert-retirement) muri porogarama mu 2017.


### Ingano y'Ibubiko


Ikindi kintu c’inguvu zo gutuma iyo porotokole itera imbere no kuyigira ishobora guhangana n’ibitero ni ukongerako ubunini bw’ibarabara ry’ibikorwa. Ico kigero kiragabanya ubushobozi bwo gukorana n’ibindi bikoresho mu gusaba ko igice cose kiba gitoyi kuruta ubu bunini. Intumbero yayo ya mbere yari iyo gukingira ibitero vy’uguhakana ibikorwa vy’ubuhinga bwa none.


Iyi parametere yongeweko mu buryo buteye ubwoba kuri kode ya Satoshi ku wa 15 Nyakanga mu buryo bw’igiharuro kidahinduka `MAX_BLOCK_SIZE` (v0.3.1), kikaba cashizwe kuri megabyte 1, 0 byte,0). Porogarama y’ugushirwa mu ngiro kw’itegeko [yakozwe] ku wa 7 Nzero n’uwaremye Bitcoin, na none ata n’itangazo ry’abantu bose ryavuye kuri we (v0.3.12). Yari itegekanije ko igipimo c'ubunini (na co nyene kigabanya umubare w'abakoresha umukono mu mabarabara) cotangura gukora kuva ku mabarabara 79.400. Ivyo vyakoreshejwe (vyabaye] ku musi wa 12 Nzero. amafaranga y’ubudandaji ku segonda, ivyo bikaba vyari bihagije cane kugira ngo bifashe mu gikorwa c’ubutunzi c’ico gihe, mbere n’inyuma y’ugucapura.


Naho Satoshi itavuze ko hariho umupaka w’ubunini bw’amabuye, abantu benshi barabonye ko uri muri kode uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Ivyo vyavuzwe rero kuva ku wa 12 Myandagaro n’umunyamuryango w’ihuriro avuga ururimi rw’ikirusiya akoresheje izina ry’uruyeri throughput [yavuze] (https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=788.msg8873#msg8873), mu buryo bushimishije ko ata wundi murongo w’ijwi, (rero umubare w'ibikorwa biri muri yo) ni muto." Mu nyuma, ku wa 30 Nzero, ni Theymos [yerekanye] uwundi munywanyi ko "Bitcoin itazokwemera amabuye arenga 1MB, rero twiyumvire ko ubunini bwa (ather1) ari buto. Bitcoin ishobora gukora gusa amafaranga 4.629 mu minota 10 yose."

Ubwa nyuma, ukubaho kw’iyi parametere biragira ico bikoze kuri Jeff Garzik [amenyesha] ko “ahagaritse umutima cane ku bijanye n’ugushobora gutera imbere kuruta guhagarika ibikorwa vya Leta” kandi uwo [abaza] ingene bishoboka "kugurisha Bitcoin ku bashoramari bakomeye, n'imipaka yubatswemwo nk'imipaka 463 ku munota." Ku bw'ivyo, ku wa 3 Gitugutu, asaba ko hoba ikindi kintu ku rubuga rwo kwongera ubunini bw'ibarabara kugera kuri 7.168 MB kugira ngo "bihure n'igipimo c'ugucuruza ca PayPal." Theymos arishura ati: "Gukoresha iki gice bizokugirira akamaro n'abandi bakiriya ba Bitcoin." Ubu butumwa bwemejwe na Satoshi Nakamoto [asaba] kudakoresha igipande kandi avuga ati: "Turashobora guhindura mu nyuma nitwaba twegereye." Uwo wa nyuma [aratomora] ivyiyumviro vyiwe umusi ukurikira mu kuyobora ingene yohindura mwene iyo porotokole.


![Message from Satoshi Nakamoto describing an increase in the block size limit in 2010](assets/en/047.webp)


Iki kiganiro ni intango y’impaka ku bijanye n’ugutera imbere, ivyo bikaba vyotuma haba intambara nyayo y’abanyagihugu hagati ya 2015 na 2017, izwi kw’izina ry’intambara y’ubunini bw’amabuye.


### Ivyitegererezo vy'inyandiko isanzwe


Muri Nzero, Satoshi na yo nyene yarashizeho iciyumviro gishasha muri iyo kode: amafaranga atari mu rugero. Ivyo ni ibikorwa ivyo ama node atunganijwe mbere y'igihe adatanga, ntabika mu mempools zayo, kandi ntashirwa mu ma blocs akora. Ariko rero, ivyo bicuruzwa biraguma bifise akamaro, kandi urubuga rwose rwemera amabuye arimwo.


Iryo tandukaniro ry’amategeko rifasha kugabanya ikoreshwa ry’ubugoyagoye bushobora kubaho mu buryo bwo kwandika bwa Bitcoin, bufise ubutunzi bwinshi kandi butasuzumwe bihagije, ku giciro c’uburenganzira bwo gukora porogarama mu gihe gito. Muri iki gihe, ubwoko bubiri bw'inyandiko z'isohoka buramenyekana nk'urugero n'urubuga:



- Ukwakira biciye ku rufunguzo rwa bose (*pubkey*), rukoreshwa n’abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro no ku bijanye no kwimurira biciye kuri IP Address;
- Ukwakira biciye ku rutoke rwa bose (*urufunguzo rwa bose Hash*), rukoreshwa mu gutanga amakuru biciye ku rufunguzo rwa Bitcoin Address.

Ku wa 7 Nzero, muri verisiyo 0.3.12, Satoshi [yarimwo](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=999.msg12240#msg12240) uburenganzira busaba ko amafaranga akoreshwa ataba manini cane, canke ngo abemwo abakoresha benshi cane b’imikono. Ivyo vyari, nk’uko yabisiguye, ugushira mu ngiro kw’intango kw’itandukaniro. Ivyo vyashizweho haciye amezi atatu na Gavin Andresen, yongeyeko kuri iyo kode igikorwa ca `IsStandard`, igikorwa kigenzura kamere y’ugucuruza. Ugushikira porogarama vyasubiwemwo mu 2012 mu gushiramwo P2SH muri porotokole.


### Ici c'iterambere


Mu ci c'umwaka w'2010, igihe hari ibintu vyinshi vyabaye, Satoshi yariyeguriye gutegura porogarama za Bitcoin. Gusohoka kw’inyandiko y’intango ya Bitcoin kuri Slashdot vyatumye habaho uruja n’uruza rw’abakoresha rudasanzwe, ivyo na vyo nyene vyatumye iyo sisitemu igira ingorane. Ku bw’ivyo, uwashinze iyo nkuru n’abamufasha (cane cane Gavin Andresen) baragerageje uko bashoboye kwose kugira ngo bakosore aho abantu bashobora guhungabana. Ariko rero, iyo nzira ntiyarokotse ikintu gikomeye, ikintu c’ugusesagura agaciro, catumye habaho uburyo bwo kugabisha burongowe na Satoshi muri iyo porogarama. Ubwa nyuma, ico kiringo cararanzwe kandi n’ukwongerwako umupaka w’ubunini bw’amabuye, ikintu nyamukuru mu mateka ya Bitcoin.


Mu mezi yakurikiye, haradutse ivyiza mu vy’ubuhinga, mu vy’ubutunzi no mu vy’ubuhinga bwa Mining, buhorobuhoro Bitcoin irahinduka umugambi w’abantu bose. "Umuryango wa Bitcoin" waraheza urabaho nk'ishirahamwe ryigenga. Ivyo tuzovyiga mu gice gikurikira c’iki cigwa.


# Umuryango wa Bitcoin

<partId>811e7c15-497a-46df-b67b-27eefbc73a63</partId>


## Urugendo rw'inzahabu rwa digitale

<chapterId>8e9899ca-e7a7-471b-8e69-847a56714d3b</chapterId>


Mu gice ca mbere, twarize ingaruka gusohora ikiganiro ca Bitcoin kuri Slashdot (slashdotting) vyagize n’ingene Satoshi n’abafasha biwe bashoboye gutorera umuti ingorane z’ubuhinga za mbere. Mu mpera z’icuma, uwo mugambi wari waratsinze iyo nkubi y’umuyaga kandi wari witeguriye kwakira abantu bariko baragwira. Mu mpera z’umwaka w’2010 rero, ni co gihe Bitcoin yaroraniwe.

Ico gihe cari igihe c’inzahabu cane cane kuri Mining, aho habonetse iterambere rikomeye n’uguseruka kw’amatongo ya mbere ya GPU n’amakoperative ya mbere. Ivyo bikoresho vyakoreshwa vyariko biragwira, kandi ubushobozi bw’ubuhinga bwa algorithme bwihariye bwariko buratera imbere. Yari nk'aho ari "urugendo rw'inzahabu rw'ubuhinga bwa none," nk'uko umuhinga mu vy'ubuhinga bwa none wo muri ico gihe (akoresheje izina ry'uruyeri jimbobway) [yanditse] avuga ko "ibihumbi vy'abakoresha internet" bari ama bitcoins ya Mining "mu cizigiro c'ubutunzi" kandi ko benshi muri bo bariko bagerageza "gutegura ibikoresho vya porogarama n'ibikoresho vyo gucukura neza ama bitcoins" mu cizigiro co kuba abatunzi b'umwanda. (*umwimerere: "Bitcoins: A New Digital Gold Rush (...) Ibihumbi vy'abakoresha Internet ubu bari Mining ku bitcoins mu cizigiro c'ubutunzi. Benshi bariko baragerageza gutegura porogarama n'ibikoresho vyo gucukura bitcoins mu buryo bwiza cane mu cizigiro co kuba abatunzi b'umwanda."*)


### Itongo rya mbere rya GPU


Inyuma y’aho Bitcoin ivuye mu kwezi kwa Nyakanga 2010, impembo nini y’amahera yava ku kwiyongera kw’igiciro be n’ubushobozi bwo gukura muri kazoza vyatumye abantu bitanga kugira ngo bakore Bitcoin cane. Ni co gituma [igipimo ca Hash](Hash](Hash](Igihe cose) c’uruja n’uruza, cari ku 0,22 GH/s ku wa 11 Nyakanga, caduze kija kuri 2,78 GH7/s ku wa 11 Nyakanga, ku wa 71 Myandagaro. 15, kugira ngo amaherezo ashike ku 9.94 GH/s ku wa 19 Nzero, amaherezo ashike ku 12.58 GH/s ku wa 29 Nzero.


![Total network hash rate from July 11 to October 5, 2010](assets/en/048.webp)

Igitigiri cose c’urubuga Hash kuva kw’igenekerezo rya 11 Nyakanga gushika kw’igenekerezo rya 5 Gitugutu 2010 (isoko: [CoinWarz]


Miner nini cane muri iki gihe yari umuhinguzi w’umudagi yagenda mw’izina rya ArtForz. Amaze kumenya ivya Bitcoin biciye kuri Slashdot, yaciye yihuta kwinjira mu gutegura porogarama, amara umwanya munini ku muhora wa IRC #Bitcoin-dev. Cane cane, yarateguye ubuhinga bwiwe bwite bwa GPU Mining akoresheje OpenCL, akabukoresha n’ikarata y’ibishushanyo ya mudasobwa yiwe.

Yatanguye gukora ama bitcoins ku wa 19 Nyakanga, ku wa 25 Nyakanga, mu rudodo rwo gukora ubushakashatsi ku bakoresha ku bijanye n’ivyo bafise Bitcoin, ArtForz . [yavuze] (https.archive.org/web/20151121004205/20151121004205/https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=564.msg5617#msg5617) yari yararonse amafaranga 1.700 mu misi 6, ivyo bikaba bihuye n’amafaranga y’amafaranga 1.700 y’amafaranga y’amafaranga y’amafaranga y’amafaranga. MH/s. Buhoro buhoro, yubatse itongo rinini rya Mining, ryari kwitwa "ArtFarm." Muri Myandagaro, itongo ryiwe [ryari ririmwo](ingene-artforz-yahinduye-amateka-ya-Bitcoin-Mining/) 6 ATI Radeon HD 5770s, bimufasha kwongerekana kuva ku wa 76 MH ku wa 40 MH/ Ubwa 13.


![ArtForz's mining production between August and October 2010](assets/en/049.webp)

Igishushanyo ca Mining ca ArtForz hagati ya Myandagaro n'Ukwakira 2010 (isoko: Blackburn n'abandi, "[Ugukorana hagati y'umugwi utazwi warakingiye Bitcoin mu gihe c'ukunanirwa kw'ugusenyura ubutegetsi](https://arxiv.org/pdf/2206.02871)")


Mu ndwi ziheze, ArtForz yaraje kugenzura igice kinini c’ububasha bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none. Ku wa 2 Nzero, Miner puddinpop [yavuze] ko afise "nk'ama 12 5770s akoresheje umukiriya wiwe wa OpenCL" kandi ko afise "ama networks arenga 1% ya G. Ubushobozi bwa Hash." (*umwimerere: "ArtForz, kuri IRC, afise nk'abantu 12 canke barenga 5770 bakoresha umukiriya wiwe bwite wa OpenCL. Urubuga rwose ruriko rurakora ikintu kiri hafi y'amasaha 5-6Ghash/s, kandi ni we wenyene yavuze ko afise amasaha arenga 1Ghash/s."*) Ku wa 23 Nzero, ArtForz [yamenyeshejwe] (ububiko bw'urubuga.org/urubuga/20180118035138/2010/09/23#l1285234390.0) y'ugufata ra63s/W2ly bigereranya 20% vy’ivyo gukora hashing. Ku wa 3 Gitugutu, bavuze ko ArtForz "ifise 20 gushika kuri 30% vy'ubushobozi bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none." (*umwimerere: "afise 20-30% vy'ububasha bwa CPU y'urubuga"*)

Ariko rero, abandi bantu bahinduye ubuhinga bwabo mu gihe c’izuba, baravyihutiye guhakana ico kibanza. Hanyuma, ArtForz buhoro buhoro yarahevye ibikorwa vya Mining kugira ngo yibande ku gutegura porogarama. Muri Myandagaro 2011, [yavuze] ko afise ubushobozi bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none butari munsi ya 1% bw’urubuga.


### Mining Ubuhinga bwihariye


Mu mpera z’umwaka w’2010, akarorero ka ArtForz karatumye abandi bacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro bihutira gutegura uburyo bwabo bwo gukora generate bitcoins n’ibikoresho vyabo vy’ugukora ibishushanyo. Kugira ngo ivyo bishoboke, abacukuzi bakoresha ibidukikije vyo gukora porogarama nka CUDA canke OpenCL. Ivyo vyatumye bashobora gushika ku bushobozi bwo guharura bupimwa mu MH/s no guserukira igice kinini c’ububasha bwose.


Ku wa 2 Nzero, Miner puddinpop [yasangira] igikoresho c’umukiriya wiwe Mining, akoresheje ubuhinga bukoresheje CUDA. Yashizemwo amafaranga 10% ku muntu wese azoyikoresha. Ubwo buryo ntibwakiriwe neza cane n’abagize ihuriro bari abashigikiye porogarama z’ubuntu.


Ku wa 6 Nzero, akurikije iciyumviro c'umunyamuryango w'ihuriro, [yavuze] ko yoba "kumbure yiteguriye guhindura kode ngo ibe inkomoko yuguruye" iyo aronka "intererano ikomeye." Ku wa 15, Jeff Garzik yaratanze [igiciro] (ivyo) ku bijanye n’ivyo, asaba guha puddinpop amafaranga 10.000 y’ama bitcoins, ayo madolari yari nk’amadolari 600 ico gihe. Puddinpop yemeye: ugucuruza kwafashe [ikibanza] (ku rutonde rw’ibintu rwari ku rwego rwa algorithme, kandi rwari rwa algorithme) [yasohowe] (yasohowe] mu gihe c’uruhusha rw’ubuntu rwa puddinpop haciye igihe gito.

Ibindi bipimo vyamenyeshejwe abantu bose nko muri ico gihe nyene. Ku wa 9 Nzero, umunyamuryango w’ihuriro yariko aragenda mw’izina rya nelisky [yasangiye] ubuhinga bwabo bwa Mining akoresheje CUDA. Ku wa 1 Gitugutu, umuntu yitwa m0mchil, yinjiye muri iyo nama muri Ruhuhuma, [yasohoye] "Gufungura CL Miner ku bantu benshi."


Ivyo vyatumye abantu bafise ubuhinga bwinshi mu vy’ubuhinga bashobora generate amafaranga menshi cane. Uretse ArtForz, Nils Schneider (tcatm) ni we yabaye umwe mu bacukuzi bakuru b’amabuye y’agaciro muri ico gihe. Ku wa 3 Gitugutu 2010, [yavuze] ko afise igipimo c’ugukora hashing c’amasegonda 983 MH/s gikozwe n’ibikoresho bitatu vy’ugukora ibishushanyo. Uwo mubare warakoze kuri Satoshi ubwiwe.


### Ivyumba vya mbere vya Mining


Ukwiyongera gukomeye kw’igipimo ca Hash kubera ubuhinga bwa Mining bwatumye gukora ama bitcoins afise processeur yo hagati bigorana, ivyo bikaba vyaciye birushiriza kugurwa. Nkako, ubushobozi bwo gutanga ama bitcoins bwaciye buvana cane n’ugutandukana, abantu bamwebamwe ntibashobora gutanga igice. Umuti w’iki kibazo ni ubufatanye Mining.


Ku wa 1 Gitugutu, m0mchil [yasohotse] (yasohotse](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=1333.msg14840#msg14840) yasanze ihinduka rya API rituma ama node y’abaguzi ashobora kugarura igice c’umukandida biciye ku gikorwa gishasha citwa if-6turwork7n. Yanditse ko iyo nzira "ifungura inzira abacukuzi bo hanze ba Bitcoin" kandi "ishobora gushinga abacukuzi benshi ku mukiriya umwe."

Kuri uwo musi nyene, iciyumviro ca "pooled Mining" caravuzwe ku ncuro ya mbere n'umunyamuryango w'ihuriro mu rudodo rwitwa "Uko twotembagaza GPU". Ku wa 13 Gitugutu, puddinpop [yasavye] ikigereranyo c’ubwo bwoko. Ubushobozi bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa Miner bupimwa n'ubuhinga bwa meta-Hash, ari bwo bucapura bw'ububiko burimwo byte ya mbere ya buri bubiko Hash. Serveri irashobora rero kugenzura ko umukiriya akora ibara ryasobanuwe. Iyi nzira iragoye kandi [ntiyemera amakosa](insiguro=1458.msg17015#msg17015).


Ariko rero, igice ca Proof of Work ni uburyo bworoshe cane bwo gupima igipimo ca Hash c’umukiriya. Ubwo buryo bwateguwe na ribuck, Nils Schneider na Gavin Andresen bakurikije insobanuro ya puddinpop. Birimwo kuronka ibimenyamenya vy’igice c’ibikorwa vy’urugero rutoyi kuruta ingorane y’uruja n’uruza rwavuye mu gice kimwe c’abahiganwa. Ivyemezo vy’ibice vyakoranijwe bituma habaho ingereranyo y’ububasha bwakoreshejwe.


Ku wa 23 Ugushyingo, verisiyo yahinduwe y’igikorwa ca `getwork` yongewe kuri [kode](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=1901.msg23876#msg23876), ku wa 25, yashizwe muri verisiyo nshasha ya porogarama nyamukuru . ([umurongo wa 0.3.17](ubutumwa bw'ibitabu.org/urutonde.php?insanganyamatsiko=1946.ubutumwa24460#ubutumwa24460)). Kuri uwo musi nyene, Jeff Garzik (uwaburanishije iciyumviro co gutandukanya uburongozi bw’uruzitiro na Mining muri porogarama) 1925.msg24217#msg24217) porogarama yiwe ya CPU Mining ikoresha iyo nzira.


Ku wa 27 Ugushyingo, umusore w’Umuceke yitwa Marek Palatinus, akoresheje izina ry’uruyeri ryitwa slush, [yasohoye] Mining" ku rubuga, ikigereranyo gikoresha `getwork` n'ubuhinga bwa Jeff Garzik. Ico kigereranyo gishingiye ku bimenyamenya vy’igice c’ibikorwa vyakozwe n’abacukuzi (pay-per-share). Bukeye, Satoshi Nakamoto [yemeje] ico ciyumviro.


![Marek Palatinus (slush) at the Z-DAY conference in Prague on May 11, 2013](assets/en/050.webp)

Marek Palatinus (umunyaruyeri) mu nama y’umusi wa Z-DAY yabereye i Prague ku wa 11 Rusama 2013


Ivyo bigereranyo bibiri vy’ugupima vyashizwe mu ngiro mu kwezi kwa kigarama. Imbere ya vyose, iciyumviro ca puddinpop carakoreshejwe ku wa 1 Kigarama n’uwukoresha incuro zibiri, uwo [yatumiye] abantu kugira ngo bahuze na server yiwe ya Mining. Iryo tsinda ryashinze igice ca mbere (95.420) ku wa 4 Kigarama. Amaze gukora iyindi block haciye imisi mikeyi, server ya doublec yarafunzwe ku wa 15. Iryo shirahamwe ryarafunze ubudasiba ku wa 17, kubera ukuza kw'ishirahamwe ry'abakozi ryiza cane: Bitcoin.cz Mining.


Amaze gukora ubushakashatsi kuri iyo nama, Marek Palatinus yaciye afata ingingo yo gushirwa mu ngiro uburyo bwiwe bwo gukorana Mining kandi cane cane akora ivyigwa ku rubuga rw’igerageza. Yarabonye kandi ko iyo server ishobora gushikirwa n’abacukuzi ba CPU (porogarama ya Jeff Garzik) n’abacukuzi ba GPU (abaguzi ba m0mchil na puddinpop).


Mu ijoro ryo kuva ku wa 15 gushika ku wa 16 Kigarama, iyo koperative yaraheza [itanguzwa] na Marek Palatinus ku rubuga rwa mbere. Igipande ca mbere [cabonetse] (97.834) mu gitondo co ku wa 16. Mu nyuma, harasohotse n’ibindi bipande vyinshi. Ishirahamwe Mining ryahuye n’uguterimbere mu ntango: mu misi mikeyi, igipimo caryo ca Hash carashitse kuri 4 GH/s, 3,5% vy’inguvu zose z’uruja n’uruza.


Iryo shirahamwe ryobaye ikigereranyo muri Bitcoin Mining. Yari afise amazina menshi mu myaka: Bitcoin Pooled Mining (BPM), Bitcoin.cz Creator Mining, n’ubwa nyuma ivyerekeye iSlush Pool. Yacitse ikidengeri c'ubwonko muri Nzero 2022.


![Logo of Slush's cooperative in September 2011](assets/en/051.webp)

Igishushanyo c’ishirahamwe rya Slush muri Nzero 2011 (inkomoko: [ububiko]


### Igitero gikomeye co gutera imbere muri Mining

Gutyo, igice ca kabiri c’umwaka w’2010 caragaragaje iterambere rikomeye kuri Mining. Yari yihariye mu kwemera ubuhinga bwa GPU (Igikoresho co Gutunganya Ivyiyumviro). Abantu benshi bariko barakora kandi bubaka amatongo nyayo ya Mining, nka ArtForz na "ArtFarm" yiwe. Ivyo vyatumye amaherezo habaho amakoperative, bituma abacukuzi batobato bashobora gukoranya ububasha bwabo bwo gukoresha ubuhinga bwa none kugira ngo bagabanye itandukaniro ry’impera.


Ariko rero, ukugwa si bwo bwonyene bwaroraniwe mu buryo bwa Mining. Vyari kandi vyiza ku kibano no ku bidukikije vy’ubutunzi, ivyo tuzobivugako mu kigabane gikurikira.


## Ugukura kw'ibidukikije

<chapterId>0404f877-8b5c-4c7f-81ab-a4e6d9b3da9c</chapterId>


Mu kigabane ca mbere, twarasuzumye ingene Mining yateye imbere mu gice ca kabiri c’umwaka w’2010. Mu mpera z’umwaka, iyo nzira yari yarashitse neza. Ariko rero, Mining si yo yonyene yari umuce wa Bitcoin waroraniwe: ibidukikije vyayo ni vyo vyaroraniwe.


Aha, tuzobanza Address intango y’ugushora Bitcoin hanze n’iterambere ry’imiryango y’Abarusiya n’Abafaransa. Tuzoheza tuganire ku bijanye n’iterambere ry’itumanaho n’iterambere ry’ubutunzi, ivyo bikaba vyatumye habaho ukwiyongera gushasha kw’igiciro ca Bitcoin. Mu gusozera, tuzovuga ibintu bibiri vy’ikigereranyo vyabaye imbere y’uko Satoshi igenda: Ukwemera kwa Bitcoin n’ishirahamwe ry’imipaka y’ubuhinga bwa none be n’ukugaruka kwa Hal Finney.


### Bitcoin mu zindi ndimi


Bitcoin ni umugambi mpuzamakungu kandi, nk’uko biri, utegerezwa gushikira abantu benshi bashoboka hanze y’aho bavuga Icongereza. Ni co gituma umuryango [wahujwe](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=151.msg1259#msg1259) watanguye muri Rusama 2010 guhindura urubuga n’igishushanyo ca porogarama Interface mu ndimi nyinshi. Igitaliyano, Ikidagi n’Igiholandi ni vyo vyari birimwo canecane.


Ariko ivyo sivyo vyose. Martti Malmi yatanguye gushinga amahuriro matomato yerekeye abatari bavuga Icongereza mu mpera z’ukwezi kwa Nyakanga. Umuryango w’Abarusiya ni wo wa mbere washinze: hakurikijwe ubusabe bwa bitcoinex kanaka, ihuriro ritoyi ry’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none [raremewe] (https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=151.msg6241#msg6241) ku wa 28 Nyakanga. threads](https://web.archive.org/web/20101018144227/20101018144227/http://www.Bitcoin.org:80/smf/index.php?board=11.0) zaremewe: Igitaliyano, Igiholandi, Igicata mu Kiyapani, n’Igitaliyani; Igisupanyoli mu kwezi kwa Nzero; n’ubwa nyuma n’ikidagi mu kwezi kwa Gitugutu. Ariko rero, nta mugwi n’umwe wari uhuye n’uw’Abarusiya, kandi ubutumwa bukeyi gusa ni bwo bwarungitswe.


Ni mu muryango w’Abafaransa ibintu vyahindukiye, cane cane biciye ku bikorwa vy’umuntu umwe: Lucien Grondin, na we nyene azwi kw’izina ry’uruyeri rya Grondilu. Ku wa 26 Nzero, yaravumbuye Bitcoin, aca ahita agira igishika ku bijanye n’uwo mugambi. Mu gicugu, yanditse [ku rubuga rwa IRC](ku rubuga rw’ububiko bw’ibintu.org/urubuga/20131201235643):4.


> "\[G\]osh sinshobora kuryama ! Nguma niyumvira ivyo bintu vyiza cane. Kuri jewe Bitcoin ni "inzahabu yo mu kirere" \[sic\]. Ndatangaye gusa."

Haciye imisi mikeyi, ku wa 30, yasohoye [amakuru](https://linuxfr.org/amakuru) mu gifaransa kuri LinuxFr.org (DLFP). Iyi nkuru, ifise umutwe uvuga ngo "Urazi ivyerekeye bitcoins?", birashoboka ko ari yo nkuru ya mbere yerekana Bitcoin yanditswe mu rurimi rwa Molière. Iyo ngingo yarashikiriye abantu benshi cane, abantu hafi 350 barayivugako. Aha niho hari paragarafu ya mbere nk’uko [yabonetse] muri ico gihe:


![Do you know about bitcoins?](assets/en/052.webp)


> **Ibitabo: Uzi bitcoin?** Bitcoin ni amafaranga y'ikoranabuhanga yatekerejwe mu 2009 n’uwitwa Satoshi Nakamoto. Aya mafaranga atandukanye n’andi mafaranga y’ikoranabuhanga kubera ko akora mu buryo butagira ugenga, peer-to-peer, kandi akoresha neza ibitekerezo by’ibanze by’ubwirinzi bwa mudasobwa. Akubiye mu porogaramu yanditswe muri C++ ikaba yasohowe ku ruhushya rwa MIT rw’ubuntu.

Cane cane, iki kiganiro gikwegera umutima w’umuntu umwe yitwa Ploum, izina ryiwe ry’ukuri Lionel Dricot, umunyabubirigi w’imyaka 29, akaba ari umunyamakuru w’ivy’ubuhinga bwa none, akaba n’umuvugizi w’ubuhinga bwa none. Ku wa 25 Gitugutu, yarasohoye ingingo ku rubuga rwiwe, yitwa "Amahera y'abanyabwenge, amahera y'inkende?", aho avugira ko ubutegetsi bwo kwegereza ubutegetsi abaturage kandi ashigikira ingingo ya Bitcoin. Benshi mu bakoresha interineti bavuga igifaransa bumvise ivyerekeye Bitcoin biciye muri ubwo buryo, harimwo [Amaury Séchet], guhingura amafaranga Bitcoin mu 2017.


![Lionel Dricot (Ploum) in 2012, then a candidate under the banner of the Pirate Party for the Belgian communal and provincial elections](assets/en/053.webp)

Lionel Dricot (Ploum) mu mwaka w’2012, ico gihe yari umukandida w’umuhari w’abasuma mu matora y’abanyagihugu n’ay’intara yo mu Bubirigi.


Uwo musi nyene, Ploum yafunguye [urudodo rw'ibiganiro] "Igifaransa" ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin. Ubutumwa buva ku bagize ihuriro bavuga igifaransa bwarongerekanye mu mezi yakurikiye. Ivyiza ni uko David François ([davout]), yanditswe ku wa 17 Gitugutu, akaba ari we azoshinga Bitcoin-Central, na Mark Karpelès ([MagicalTux]), yanditswe ku wa 7 Ugushyingo kandi azoba nyen’urubuga rwa Mt. Gox, yari muri iyo nama. Yarabonye kandi uruhara rw’umuntu yitwa Jean-Luc yari gufungura urubuga [Bitcoin.fr](https://web.archive.org/web/20110107145746/) ku wa 23 Kigarama gushika ku wa 2019. [guteza imbere] (gutera imbere] (its: 1567. ubutumwa37524#ubutumwa37524) it muri Mukakaro. Ihuriro ry'igifaransa ryoheza ryaremewe na Martti Malmi kw'igenekerezo rya 1 Ruhuhuma 2011.


### Iterambere ry'Itumatumanako

Uretse uguteza imbere imiryango y’indimi, hariho n’ubuhinga bushasha mu buryo bukoreshwa mu guhanahana amakuru ku bijanye na Bitcoin. Ku wa 4 Gitugutu, umunya Australiya w’imyaka 38 akoresheje izina ry’uruyeri ryitwa noagendamarket [yatanguje] umugambi witwa BitcoinMedia. Guteza imbere Bitcoin mu guhingura ibirimwo no kubimenyekanisha mu bibanza bishobora gukwegera abantu ni co ciyumviro. Naho iyo ngingo itashitse ku co yari yiteze, irafise akamaro ko gutuma hakorwa amavidewo ya mbere avuga ivyerekeye Bitcoin. Videwo ya mbere y’uwo muhora, [yasohowe](yasohowe](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=1355.msg15461#msg15461) ku wa 5 Gitugutu, ni Inkuru y’Ugushakashaka kuri Google, yakozwe hakoreshejwe igikoresho ca YouTube (raba ifoto iri musi). Ayandi mavidewo azokorwa hakoreshejwe Xtranormal, igikoresho coroshe co guhingura urutonde rw’amavidewo bivuye ku bimenyetso n’imiterere vyategekanijwe imbere y’igihe.


![First video on Bitcoin (Google Search Story)](assets/en/054.webp)


Ivyo bimenyetso vyerekeye Bitcoin biriko biragwira muri iki kiringo. Ivyo ni ko biri cane cane kuri Jon Matonis, afise urubuga *The Monetary Future* aho avuga ku mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none, ubuhinga bwo gukoresha amabanki ku buntu, n’ubuhinga bwo gukora amakuru y’ubuhinga bwa none. Yavumbuye Bitcoin muri Ntwarante maze [arahindura](ubutumwa-bwanje-bwa mbere-kuri-GW6#48) yatanguye kwandika kuri iyo nkuru. Mu kwezi kwa Gitugutu, arasohora [ingingo ya gatatu](https://themonetaryfuture.blogspot.com/2010/10/rally-in-Bitcoin.html) aho avuga ibijanye n’ukwiyongera kw’ibiciro, akavuga n’ibintu bishasha vyo mu bidukikije.


![Profile picture of Jon Matonis in 2011](assets/en/055.webp)

Ifoto ya Jon Matonis mu mwaka w'2011 (isoko: [Forbes]


Muri iki gihe, ikimenyetso gishasha ca Bitcoin na co nyene carashikirijwe. Ku wa 1 Ugushyingo, umunyamuryango w’ihuriro akoresheje izina ry’uruyeri bitboy [yasohowe] (https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=1631.0) igishushanyo Elements kugira ngo yerekane amafaranga y’ibanga. Imwe muri izo Elements ni ikimenyetso c’umuhondo gifise urudome B rwaciweko kandi rwinjiye gatoyi:


![Bitcoin logo designed by bitboy, November 2010](assets/en/056.webp)


### Ubutunzi buriko burakura

Ico kiringo kandi kirangwa n’iterambere ridasanzwe ry’ibidukikije ku rugero rw’ubutunzi. Mu mpera z’umwaka w’2010, hariho amabarabara nka Mt. Gox, Bitcoin Market, n’ayandi, ariko ivyo ntivyari bihagije. Uko ni ko amafaranga y’ubudandaji atangura kugwira. Uretse uguhanahana amakuru gukorwa biciye ku butumwa bwihariye ku rubuga, hariho uburyo bukomeye gatoyi: #Bitcoin-otc. Ni umurongo wa IRC kuri Freenode [wafunguwe](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=1491.msg17508#msg17508) n’uwukoresha aja mw’izina nanotube ku wa 18 Gitugutu. urubuga](web.archive.org/web/20101027090714) kandi uguhanahana bibera ata guca ku ruhande hagati y’ababiri, ata n’amahera yo gushiramwo, biciye mu buryo butandukanye bwo kwishura (PayPal, Liberty). Igitigiri c’ibikorwa vyemeza Bitcoin na co nyene kiraduga, naho coba kiguma ari gito cane, nk’uko [vyemezwa] n’urubuga rwemewe rw’urutonde rw’ibintu vy’ubudandaji.

Ivyo vyose Elements bituma igiciro kiduga cane. Naho nyene ryahagaze hafi y’ibice 6¢ kuva mu kwezi kwa munani, ritangura kuduga mu ntango z’ukwezi kwa Gitugutu. Ija ku 10¢, igashika ku 20¢ mu mpera z’ukwezi. Ku wa 6 Ugushyingo, rirenga 50¢, ivyo bikaba bitabura [gutera umunezero] abagize ihuriro.


![BTC Price between July 18 and October 18, 2010 on Mt. Gox](assets/en/057.webp)

Igiciro ca BTC hagati y’italiki 18 Nyakanga n’italiki 18 Gitugutu 2010, ku musozi Gox (isoko: [*Igihe kizoza c’amahera*](https://akazoza k’amahera.


Kuduga kwa Bitcoin bisigura ko ibintu bitangura gupimwa, haba mu bijanye n’igiciro, igikorwa ku ruzitiro, canke Mining. Abantu bose barazi ko ibidukikije biriko birakura, ariko nta n’umwe azi ingene yobigereranya neza. Ni co gituma ibikorwa vyavutse mu gice ca kabiri c’umwaka w’2010 no mu ntango z’umwaka w’2011, muri vyo harimwo ivy’ingenzi harimwo:



- Bitcoin Watch ([ububiko bw'ibitabu.com/urubuga/20100816161306/)), igikoresho co gukoranya imibare [vyateguwe] na Jeff Garzik (jgarzik);
- Ibishushanyo vya Bitcoin ([ibishushanyo vy'ibiciro vy'ibice. [yatangujwe] na Nils Schneider (tcatm) ku wa 4 Ugushyingo;
- Bitcoin Block explorer ([ububiko bw'ibintu.com/urubuga/20101128030227/ububiko bw'ibintu. up](htps.21124) na Theymos ku wa 10 Ugushyingo, bituma umuntu wese ashobora gushika ku birimwo amabuye ya Bitcoin n’ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji akoresheje umucukumbuzi w’urubuga;
- Ivyerekana urubuga rwa Bitcoin ([Bitcoin.sipa.be]), urubuga rwerekana ibishushanyo vy’iterambere ry’urubuga rwa GW-6099 GW- [yatangujwe] na Pieter Wuille (sipa) ku wa 28 Nzero 2011;
- Bitcoin Monitor ([bitcoinmonitor.com]), igikoresho co gukurikirana mu gihe nyaco c’ibikorwa, amabuye, n’ibikorwa vya Exchange, [shiramwo na Jan Vornberger (jav) ku wa 6 Ruhuhuma 2011.


Ikintu ca nyuma kigaragaza ko Bitcoin yaroraniwe ni uko bamwebamwe barondeye kugerageza aho igarukira. Abantu ku giti cabo bararyohewe hagati y’igenekerezo rya 15 n’irya 26 Munyonyo mu kurema umwuzure w’amahera, akaba ari ibihumbi ku musi. Ico gikorwa kidasanzwe [cavuzwe] ku wa 19 na Jeff Garzik. Yatumye Satoshi ishira mu ngiro ingingo, mu [gusubizaho] amafaranga y’ugucuruza Interface no kwongerako imipaka ku gucuruza ku buntu.


### Ishirahamwe ry’imipaka y’ubuhinga bwa none ryemera Bitcoin


Mu mpera z'umwaka w'2010, ikintu gihambaye cabaye ni uko ishirahamwe ry'imipaka y'ubuhinga bwa none ryemeye Bitcoin. Iryo shirahamwe ni ishirahamwe mpuzamakungu ry’ugukingira umwidegemvyo kuri Internet, ryashinzwe mu 1900 na Mitch Kapor, John Gilmore na John Perry Barlow. Ivyo vyari bihambaye canecane ku bantu ba mbere bakoresheje Bitcoin, bakaba bari aba cypherpunks mu mutima. Bari bafise umutima ukunze wo kwemera Bitcoin.


![Logo of the Electronic Frontier Foundation](assets/en/058.webp)


Ni umunyamuryango w’ihuriro yitwa Kiba yafashe ingingo ku wa 13 Myandagaro 2010, mu [gusaba](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=804.msg9021#msg9021) guhamagara EFF no gusaba ko bemera intererano, [vyakoranijwe] (ivy’ubuhinga bwa none) bivuye mu kibano. Ku bw’ivyo, yashizeho [konti](konti] kuri MyBitcoin aho yakoranirije ayo mahera kandi yipfuza gutanga uburenganzira bwo gushika muri EFF. Yarateguye email (yakosowe n’abanyagihugu) yohereje mu mpera z’ukwezi kwa munani.


Uwugira kabiri wo muri iyo nama yaraje kumufasha haciye indwi zibiri, ata n’umwe yishuye. Uwo munywanyi akoresheje izina ry’uruyeri BrightAnarchist, yari azi umwe mu bashinze iyo sosiyete maze abarungikira ubutumwa kuri e-mail ku wa 13 Nzero. Iyo nkuru yaciye ishikirizwa ishirahamwe.


EFF yafashe umwanya kugira ngo itangure kwemera intererano za bose. Inyuma y’ibiganiro, abarundi barabemeje gutangaza intererano Address ku rubuga rwabo. Ku wa 9 Ugushyingo, igitabu Address carabonetse kuri [urupapuro rw’intererano]. Abakoresha Bitcoin [batanguye] gutanga amahera.


Haciye imisi mikeyi, [ivyo] vyanditswe ku rubuga rwa jimbo Bitcoin. Iyi nkuru [yasangiwe] ku rubuga rwa HackerNews. Ivyo vyanditswe kandi mu masanamu na BitcoinMedia ikoresheje Xtranormal:


:::id ya videwo=03dfd302-1e05-4cad-a91a-e5e65f1d0932:::


Iyi ni inkuru nziza cane kuri Bitcoin kuko izo nzira zompi zisangiye agaciro. Ikindi kandi, EFF izwi cane mu gutanga uburinzi bushingiye ku mategeko ku migambi yo kuzigama ubuzima bwite no gusangira amakuru nka Tor na BitTorrent. Satoshi Nakamoto ubwiwe arabizi kandi arashigikiye cane cane ibikorwa vy’ishirahamwe, nk’uko vyerekanwa mu [vyiyumviro] vyiwe(https://mmalmi.github.io/Satoshi/#email-254) yandikiye muri imwe mu ma email yandikiye Gavin Andresen ku wa 6 Nzero 2019.

> "EFF irahambaye cane. Turashaka kuguma dufitaniye ubucuti bwiza na bo. Ni twebwe umugambi bashima; barafashije umugambi wa TOR kandi bakoze vyinshi mu kurinda gusangira amadosiye ya P2P."

### Ukugaruka kwa Hal Finney


Amaze kuva muri Bitcoin muri Ndamukiza 2009, Hal Finney yaciye amenya ningoga ko yasuzumwe indwara ya ALS, iyo ndwara ikaba yariko irasuzumwa muri Myandagaro 2009.


Ku wa 30 Ugushyingo, aca yiyandikisha ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin maze atangura kuja mu biganiro, cane cane ivyerekeye umugambi wa BitDNS. Ntatinya gutanga amahera ku migambi itandukanye itera imbere mu bidukikije.


Ikindi kandi, ariga iyo kode, iyo ataravye kuva itanguye, agaca abona ibikorwa vyose vyakozwe. Ivyo bimutera kwandika ibi bikurikira ku nama yo ku wa 11 Kigarama:

> "Iki kimeze nk'akazi keza cane, naho nipfuza ko hoba hariho ibindi bivugwa. Narize cane cane init, main, script, n'ibindi bice vy'urubuga. Iyi ni imashini ikomeye."

Haciye amasaha abiri, Satoshi [inyishu] (insiguro=2188.ubutumwa29259#ubutumwa29259):

> "Ivyo bisigura vyinshi biva kuri wewe, Hal. Urakoze."

Ivyo rero vyari ubutumwa bwa nyuma bwa mbere bwavuye ku muremyi wa Bitcoin, yari kuzimangana haciye amezi makeyi.


### Igihe gihambaye

Mu mpera z’umwaka w’2010, ibidukikije bikikuje Bitcoin vyarateye imbere cane. Ivy’uguhanahana amakuru vyarateye imbere, ubutunzi na bwo buratera imbere. Iciyo gihe, indege Bitcoin yasa n’iyiteguriye guhaguruka yonyene. Muri ico kiringo nyene niho Satoshi yahisemwo kuzimangana, igasiga uburongozi bw’uwo mugambi ku baturage.


## Ukuzimangana kwa Satoshi

<chapterId>f7735239-4887-468f-9f06-1b07d00b30d9</chapterId>


Twarabonye ingene Bitcoin yafashe indege inyuma y’aho ico canditswe gisohokeye kuri Slashdot muri Nyakanga 2010. Kubera iterambere ritandukanye mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwa none, Mining, n’ubutunzi mu mpera z’umwaka, amaherezo uwo mugambi wari mu nzira nziza. Ni co gituma ico kiringo cahuye n’igihe Satoshi Nakamoto yariko irasohoka buhoro buhoro.


Ugusohoka kw’umuremyi wa Bitcoin kwatumwe n’imvo zibiri: ku ruhande rumwe, ingorane ziriko zirakura ku bijanye n’ikibanza ciwe, zisaba ko uburongozi bugenda bwegerejwe kandi bushingiye ku kwumvikana; ku rundi ruhande, ubwoba yari afise hafi y’ugutinya abategetsi ba Leta. Ico ciyumviro ca nyuma caragaragajwe cane cane mu kwezi kwa kigarama 2010 mu gihe WikiLeaks yari yabujijwe amafaranga, iyo na yo ikaba itagishobora kuronka amahera biciye mu buryo bwa kera, kandi Bitcoin yari yarayihaye uburyo bundi bubereye. Muri iki kigabane, tuzodondora mu buryo burambuye ingene iyo nzira y’ukuzimangana yagenda.


### Ingorane ku bijanye n'Ikibanza c'Umushingwamanza


Kuva mu gice ca kabiri c’umwaka w’2010, umuryango w’iterambere warakoraniye ku muhora #Bitcoin-dev, ivyo bitabo vyawo bikaba bisohoka ku rubuga rwa Christian Decker, [Bitcoin]. Imibare](urubuga.ububiko.org/urubuga/20131201235340/urubuga.imibare.com/irc/Bitcoin-dev/logs/2010/09). Iyi nzira yari ahantu heza cane ku bantu bamenye neza ivy’ubuhinga kugira ngo bashobore kumenya ido n’ido ryerekeye Bitcoin no kuganirako mu buryo butamenyerewe. Yahuje abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro b’abahinga (nka ArtForz, Diablo-D3, knightmb, canke Nils Schneider), abahinguzi bakunda iyo porotokole (nka Gavin Andresen, Jeff Garzik, canke Wladimir van der Laan), canke abantu babungabunga ibikorwa kuri Bitcoin (nka Jed, Marquard, Michael canke Michael).


Ariko rero, Satoshi Nakamoto ntiyigeze ayifatanya na yo, rero imvugo yo ng’aho yari yidegemvya kuruta iyo mu nama. Kenshi vyarabaye ko ingingo za Satoshi zo guteza imbere zishirwako ibibazo canke mbere ikibanza ciwe ku bijanye na Bitcoin kiganegurwa.

Satoshi ni we murongozi w'uwo mugambi, ivyo bizwi mw'isi y'ubuhinga bwa none nk'"[Umunyagitugu w'Ubuntu ku Buzima](https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Umunyagitugu w'Ubuntu_w'Ubuzima)." Uruhara rwiwe ni ugutuma iterambere ry’abantu bose riguma rihagaze mu gufata ingingo ku muntu wese, ivyo bikaba bigabanya ingorane z’ubugarariji n’amacakubiri. Nk'uko [vyasiguwe] na Gavin Andresen, ni we "murinzi w'irembo": "amakode yose aca muri we."


Ariko rero, kode y’inkomoko ya Bitcoin iguma ari ubuntu, ku buryo umuntu wese ashobora kuyikopa no kuyihindura, ivyo bikaba bibuza ko ugutera imbere kw’iyo porotokole kuba ataco bimaze. Nk’uko vyavuzwe na Jeff Garzik ku wa 19 Ugushyingo:


> "Satoshi yaje n'imibare y'ubupfumu ivuye mu kirere gitoyi, kandi twese hamwe turashigikira iyo nzira. [...] Umunota Satoshi ikora ikintu c'ubusazi kidashigikirwa n'abanyagihugu ni igihe amategeko / urutonde rw'amategeko ruhinduka vy'ukuri."

Gutyo, uruhara rwa Satoshi nk’umurongozi ntirubuza ko abantu bamunegura. Ni co gituma buhoro buhoro amahane aza mu kibano guhera mu kwezi kwa Nyakanga. Nk’akarorero, ukurwanya biravyuka mu gihe c’[ugushirwaho] kw’uburyo bwo kugabisha muri Myandagaro canke mu kwezi kwa 10745. [uguhindura](ihindura] (ihinduka] (ihinduka ry'ibikorwa) ry'igikorwa ca m0mchil `getwork` mu kwezi kwa 11. Intimba ku bijanye n’iyo ngingo y’ubutegetsi bw’igitugu rimwe na rimwe iraserurwa [mu buryo bugaragara cane](https://buildingbitcoin.org/Bitcoin-dev/log-2010-11-24.html#l-384) kuri IRC.


Gavin, ari hafi cane ya Satoshi ariko kandi akayaga n’abandi bategura, arabona neza ingorane iterwa n’ivyo bintu. Ku wa 27 Nzero 2010, kuri IRC, Gavin [yamenyesheje] ko yoshima "gushobora kwemeza \[Satoshi guhindura uburyo bwo gukorana." (*umwimerere: "Nipfuza gusa kumujijura ngo ahindure akaja ku buryo bwo guteza imbere ubufatanye."*) Mu kwezi kwa Gitugutu, Gavin [aronka](https://sourceforge.net/p/Bitcoin/code/165/) kwandika uburenganzira bwo gushika ku bubiko bwa SourceForge, akagira ibintu vyiza. Mu kwezi kwa kigarama, iyo ngorane yaratowe umuti igihe Satoshi yasohoka bukwi na bukwi inyuma y’aho ikibazo ca WikiLeaks giturikiye.

### Ikibazo ca WikiLeaks


Ico catumye Satoshi igenda ni ikibazo ca WikiLeaks. WikiLeaks ni ishirahamwe ritagira aho rigarukira ryashinzwe na Cypherpunk Julian Assange mu 2006, rigamije guha ijwi abamenyesha amakuru n’abatanga amakuru mu gihe bariko barinda aho bava. Mu mwaka w’2010, izo nyandiko z’ibanga zahishuwe n’iryo shirahamwe ry’abanyagihugu zarashikirijwe n’ibinyamakuru bikomeye, zituma abantu benshi bavyiyumvira. Ivyo bihangayikishije cane cane ibikorwa birenze urugero vy’igisirikare ca Amerika, nk’ugupfa kw’abasivile n’ibikorwa vy’ugucumukura vyakozwe, muri Afghanistan (Afghan War Diary) no muri Iraki (Iraq War Logs).


![WikiLeaks logo in November 2010](assets/en/059.webp)


Infashanyo WikiLeaks itanga ishingiye ahanini ku ntererano za bose, ni co gituma ishirahamwe ryizigira abajejwe kwishura kugira ngo baronke amahera kuri internet. Ariko rero, hakurikijwe ivyo bimenyetso, abo bahuza barashirwako umukazo batinya ingene umugenzuzi azovyifatamwo. Ni co gituma ishirahamwe ry'ugutanga amahera kuri internet ryitwa Moneybookers [rihagarika] konti y'iryo shirahamwe ry'abanyagihugu ku wa 14 Gitugutu.


Ivyo bica bifungura inzira y’ubwami yo gukoresha Bitcoin, idashingiye ku muntu wa gatatu yizigirwa kandi yoshobora kunanira neza cane ugucengera ivy’amahera. Mu kwezi kwa 11, Amir Taaki, umwongereza w’imyaka 22 w’umunyairani akoresha izina ry’uruyeri ryitwa genjix, ni we yatanguje iyo nkuru ku bijanye n’ihuriro.


![Amir Taaki in December 2012 in Bratislava](assets/en/060.webp)

Amir Taaki mu kwezi kwa kigarama 2012 i Bratislava (isoko: [Mitch Altman]))


Umunyaruyeri, umunyagitugu, akaba n’umukinyi w’umupira w’amaguru), aherutse kumenya ivyerekeye ikigereranyo ca Satoshi Nakamoto. Abona mu vyo WikiLeaks irimwo ari akaryo ko kwerekana akamaro ka Bitcoin. Ku wa 10 Ugushyingo, [yanditse] ubutumwa bukurikira kuri iyo nama:


> "Nashaka kohereza ikete kuri Wikileaks ku bijanye na Bitcoin kuko ikibabaje ni uko bagize ibintu vyinshi vyabaye aho amahera yabo yafashwe mu bihe vya kera. [...] Hari uwuzi aho yobarungikira ubutumwa?"

Ivyo abantu bavuga kuri ico ciyumviro biratandukanye. [Dukurikije] umukoresha umwe (ShadowOfHarbringer), "ivyo bishobora kuba vyiza kuri wikileaks, ariko si ngombwa ko ari vyiza kuri Bitcoin." Uwundi (creighto) [yanditse] ko "uko bigenda biraza niko bigenda neza. Uko intwaro zimara igihe kirekire zitegereje gukora, ni ko urubuga rwa Bitcoin rukomera, kandi ni ko rukomeza gutera ingorane."


Haciye indwi nkeyi, ku wa 3 Kigarama, PayPal yafashe ingingo yo guhagarika konti ya WikiLeaks maze isohora [itangazo](itangazo ry’urubuga rwa interineti. Bukeye mu gitondo, umuhinga mu vy’ubuhinga Wladimir van der Laan [atangaza] aya makuru ku rubuga:


> "Paypal yarababujije, kandi bariko baragerageza gutuma n'ayandi mabanki yo muri Amerika akora nk'ukwo nyene. Ico coba ari igihe ciza co gufungura intererano za Bitcoin."
Ukwo guhinduka kw’ibintu biratuma iyo mpari irushiriza gukomera. Umuntu umwe cane cane ashigikiye ko WikiLeaks yemera Bitcoin: Robert S. Horning, umuhinga mu vy’urudandazwa rwa mudasobwa aba muri Utah, akaba ari umuhinga mu vy’ubuhinga bwa none, kandi akaba ari we yashizeho umusanzu kuri Wikipedia, Mukakaro. Uwo musi, yanditse igisomwa kirekire asigura ko gushigikira WikiLeaks ari ukuri mu vy’inyifato runtu kandi ko Leta izokwumva ivya Bitcoin vuba canke bidatevye uko biri kwose. Aca asozera ati:

> "Mu bisanzwe, muzane. Reka turemeshe Wikileaks gukoresha Bitcoins kandi nditeguye guhangana n'ingorane iyo ari yo yose canke ingaruka mbi zivuye muri ico gikorwa."

### Ugusohoka bukwi na bukwi kw'indege Satoshi


Satoshi ntaco asangiye na Robert Horning kandi arwanya guteza imbere Bitcoin ku rubuga rwa WikiLeaks. Nk’uko amajambo yiwe n’ibikorwa vyiwe bivyemeza, aragira ubwitonzi bwinshi ku bijanye n’ubutegetsi bwa Leta, rimwe na rimwe akagera ku [paranoia] (https://mmalmi.github.io/Satoshi/#email-158). Ku bw’ivyo, ku wa 5 Kigarama, aca yishura kuri uwo mutima mu [kwishura] (https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=1735.msg26999#msg26999) bimwe bikomeye ku murongozi mukuru:


> "Oya, ntu 'bizane'.
>

> Umugambi urakeneye gukura buhoro buhoro kugira ngo software ishobore gukomezwa mu nzira.
>

> Ndasaba WikiLeaks ngo ntigerageze gukoresha Bitcoin. Bitcoin ni umuryango mutoyi wa beta mu ntango zawo. Ntiwoshobora guhagarara ngo uronke ibirenze ivyo guhindura mu mufuko, kandi ubushuhe wozana bwoshobora kudusenyura muri iki gihe."

Mu misi ikurikira, haratunganijwe uburenganzira nyabwo bwo guhagarika amahera kuri WikiLeaks, harimwo Mastercard na Visa, ariko kandi na Western Union, Bank of America, n’abandi bafatanyabikorwa, ivyo bikaba [bitera ingorane](https://wikileaks.org/Banking-Blockade.html) ubuzima bw’amahera bw’ishirahamwe ritagira aho rigarukira. Ico gitero gituma kwemera Bitcoin biba vyiza cane, kandi ico ciyumviro kirakwiragira mu buryo busanzwe.


Ku wa 11 Kigarama, ingingo yerekana ko Bitcoin ishobora gukoreshwa na WikiLeaks [yasohowe] guharura. Ico canditswe, canditswe n'umunyamakuru [Keir Thomas](https://www.keirthomas.com/ingene-natumye-uwo-muhungu-wa-Bitcoin-aja-kwihisha/), gifise umutwe uvuga ngo "Mbega ikibazo ca Wikileaks coshobora gutuma haba amafaranga mashasha y'ubuhinga bwa none?". Isanduku ya Pandora irafungurwa: ingingo ya PC World izosomwa n’abantu benshi, harimwo bishoboka ko ari abayobozi ba WikiLeaks, bituma iyo NGO yihweza ubu buryo bwo kwishura. Iyo nkuru iravugwa ningoga ku rubuga, kandi ingene umuremyi wa Bitcoin yavyifashemwo nta gukeka. We [yanditse] (Ikiganiro=2216.ubutumwa29280#ubutumwa29280):


> "Vyari vyiza ko ivyo bimenyekana mu bundi buryo bwose. WikiLeaks yarateye urusenga rw'inzoka, kandi iyo nkoko iriko iraza aho turi."

Umusi ukurikira, Satoshi [asohora] ubutumwa bwiwe bwa nyuma ku rubuga, amenyesha ko hasohotse verisiyo nshasha y’ugutegura porogarama (v0.3.of improvice-service- ibitero. Hanyuma, akava mu vyo abantu bamubona, akayaga gusa mu mwiherero n’abo bakorana hafi cane.


Mu misi yakurikiye, iyo nkuru yasohotse kuri PC World yarafise ingaruka zayo. Ku wa 14 Kigarama, ubuhinga bwa Satoshi buravugwa n’ishirahamwe ry’imipaka y’ubuhinga bwa none mu [canditswe](https://www.eff.org/deeplinks/2010/12/ibikorwa-vy’ubwubatsi-vy’ukurwanya-ugucengera) ku bijanye n’ugucengera kw’ishirahamwe rya WikiLeaks [ gusobanura](Bitcoin-intambwe-ija-ku-guhangana n'ugucengera) Bitcoin nk'"ifaranga ry'ubuhinga bwa none ry'uguhangana n'ugucengera"). Ku wa 23, amafaranga y’ibanga [aravugwa] ku rubuga rwa Keizer, ikiganiro c’ivy’ubutunzi catunganijwe na Stacy Herbert the Russia channel na Sta. Ivyasohotse kuri Wiki. Ivyo binyamakuru bituma abantu barushiriza kwitwararika cane Bitcoin, ivyo bikaba vyemeza ubwoba Satoshi yari afise.


### Ugutanga uburenganzira bwo kuronka n'imeli za nyuma

Kuva mu ntango z’ukwezi kwa kigarama, Satoshi yaratanguye gutegura ukuntu azomukurikira. Kubera ko yari afise umugambi wo kuvayo, canke n’imiburiburi gusubira inyuma, yari akeneye guha amabanga atandukanye abantu yizigira, cane cane Martti Malmi na Gavin Andresen. Ariko rero, ntiyigeze ababwira mu buryo butomoye umugambi wiwe.


Ubwa mbere, yashaka kwongerako aderesi zabo za e-mail ku [paji yo guhamagara](https://web.archive.org/web/20101215111454/http://www.Bitcoin.org/contact) y’urubuga. Ku wa 7 Kigarama, [yarungikiye](https://mmalmi.github.io/Satoshi/#email-245) ubutumwa kuri Martti amusaba nimba yoshobora "kumushira ku rutonde rw'abategura umugambi kuri paji yo guhamagara," ivyo uwo musore w'umu Finlande yaremeye. Uwaremye Bitcoin yarasavye Gavin ivyo nyene, na we nyene aravyemera. Satoshi yongeyeko amaderesi yabo kuri iyo paji, akuraho ayawe. Gavin [yovuga] haciye imyaka mikeyi:


> "\[Satoshi\] yarangije ankwegakwega yihuta mu kubaza nimba yoshobora gushiramwo imeyili yanje Address kuri paji y'intango ya Bitcoin, nanje ndamubwira ngo ego, ntazi ko iyo ashize imeyili yanje Address ng'aho, yotwara ivyiwe."

Ariko ivyo sivyo vyose. Satoshi na we nyene yashaka guha Gavin Andresen ububasha bwiwe bwo kugenzura iyo porogarama. Gavin, yari amaze guhabwa uburenganzira bwo kwandika ububiko kuri SourceForge [mu kwezi kwa Gitugutu](https://sourceforge.net/p/Bitcoin/code/165/), ni we yabaye umucungerezi mukuru w’ububiko. Ku wa 19 Kigarama, [yaremye] ububiko kuri GitHub, birashoboka ko yumva ameze neza cane na Git. Uwo musi nyene, yaranditse ubutumwa burebure kuri iyo nama asigura ko azorushiriza kwitabira iterambere. Yamenyesheje:


> "N'umuhezagiro wa Satoshi, kandi n'umutima ukunze, ngiye gutangura gukora cane uburongozi bw'umugambi wa Bitcoin."

Satoshi yahaye ububasha bwo kugenzura urubuga, ihuriro, na wiki Martti, yari asanzwe ari we arongoye izo Elements. Maze mu mpera z’umwaka wa 2011, arazimangana ata kabuza.

Mu bantu ba nyuma bavuganye na Satoshi harimwo na Mike Hearn, injeniyeri wa Google yari yamushikiriye imyaka ibiri imbere y’aho. Hearn yongeye gukorana n’uwaremye Bitcoin mu kwezi kwa kigarama 2010 kugira ngo amubaze ibindi bibazo vy’ubuhinga. Yariko arakora ku "gushirwa mu ngiro kwa Java kw'igenzura ry'ukwishyura ryoroshe, afise ijisho ryo kwubaka umukiriya akoresha amatelefone ya Android." (*umwimerere: "Nariko ndakora ku bijanye n'ugushirwa mu ngiro kwa Java kw'igenzura ry'ukwishyura ryoroshe, mfise ijisho ryo kwubaka umukiriya akoresha amatelefone Android."*) Abo bagabo babiri barahanahana ubutumwa gushika ku wa 23 Ndamukiza. Satoshi yatangaje ko "yagiye mu bindi bintu" kandi ko Bitcoin "yari mu maboko meza na Gavin n'abandi." (*original: "Naciye nsubira mu bindi. Biri mu maboko meza na Gavin n'abandi bose."*).


Ku wa 26 Ndamukiza 2011, Satoshi yararungikiye Gavin [ubutumwa bwa nyuma](http://gavinandresen.ninja/imyaka-cumi n’umwe-iheze-uyu musi) biciye kuri email, aho yanditse ati:


> "Nifuza ko utoguma uvuga kuri jewe nk'umuntu w'igitutu w'akabanga, itangazamakuru rihindura ivyo mu mfuruka y'amahera y'abasuma. Kumbure ahubwo ubigire ku mugambi w'inkomoko yuguruye maze ushire hejuru abagufasha; birafasha kubatera intege."

Aha, Satoshi yariko yerekeza ku [ngingo] (http.forbes.com/forbes/2011/0509) yasohowe ku rubuga rwa Forbes mu kwezi kwa 2011. umuntu afise umutima w’ubuzima bwite" (*umwimerere: "umuntu w’akabanga, afise umutima w’ubuzima bwite"*) kandi aho Bitcoin yashizwe ahabona nk’uburyo bwo kuronka ibiyayuramutwe bitemewe n’amategeko (vy’ukuri, ico ni co gihe urubuga rwa Silk Road rwatanguye kuroranirwa). Mu rwandiko yandikiye Gavin, Satoshi na we nyene yarashizeko urufunguzo rwo kugabisha, rwoshobora gukoreshwa mu kugabisha urubuga ku bibazo vy’ubuhinga.


Ubwa nyuma, mu ntango za Rusama, na we nyene yarasezeye Martti. Amajambo ya nyuma yabwiye umuntu wiwe wa mbere w’iburyo ni aya:


> "Narimukiye mu bindi bintu kandi kumbure sinzoba ndiho muri kazoza."
> Inzahabu y’Igihugu p. 81

### CIA, WikiLeaks, na EFF

Ku wa 26 Ndamukiza 2011, Gavin Andresen yararungikiye indege Satoshi Nakamoto [imeli ya nyuma], iyo ndege ntiyayishuye. Muri iyo email, [yerekanye] (http://gavinandresen.ninja/imyaka-cumi n’imwe-iheze-uyu musi) ko yatumiwe na In-Q-Tel, ikigega c’abanyamerika gicungera CIA, kugira ngo yerekane Bitcoin. Yari azi neza ingene uru rugendo rwovyifatamwo generate, ariko afata ingingo yo kugenda uko biri kwose. Yarashingira intahe ingingo yiwe mu kwandikira Satoshi ati:


> "Nizigiye ko mu kuvugana na bo, kandi ikiruta vyose, kwumviriza ibibazo vyabo, bazokwiyumvira Bitcoin nk'uko nanje mbibona- nk'amahera meza, akora neza, adashingiye ku vyipfuzo vya politike. Si nk'igikoresho c'isoko ry'umwirabura gikomeye cane."

Bukeye, Gavin [yamenyesheje] amakuru yari ku rubuga rw’ihuriro mu buryo buboneka. Yaciye asobanura neza ko yarihevye amadolari 3.000 y’Amerika kubera urwo rugendo. Ariko ivyo ntivyavyuriye umutima mu kibano, kuko catahura uburyo yakoresha, naho nyene vyari bikwiye ko batizigirana. Urugendo rwa Gavin ku cicaro gikuru ca CIA [rwabaye] ku wa 14 Ruheshi.


Mu buryo bw’ikigereranyo, igenekerezo rya 14 Ruheshi ni ryo kandi itariki WikiLeaks [yatanguriyeko] kwemera intererano za Bitcoin. Iyi nkuru yashizwe ku rubuga rwa Forbes.


Ikibabaje ni uko iyo nkuru yasubije inyuma igice c’ukwemera kwariho kw’ishirahamwe: Ishirahamwe ry’Imipaka y’Ikoranabuhanga. Ku wa 20 Ruheshi, EFF [yatangaje] ko vy’ukuri ihevye intererano za Bitcoin, kubera ingorane z’amategeko ivyo kwemera vyari birimwo. Yarasubije amahera yaronse kuri Bitcoin Faucet ya Gavin Andresen. Gutyo, Bitcoin yararonse ishirahamwe rimwe kubera irindi.


### Ibanga rya Satoshi

Gutyo, ukuzimangana kwa Satoshi kwabaye bukwi na bukwi hakurikijwe iterambere ry’abanyagihugu inyuma y’ugutera ivyatsi (slashdotting) kandi ikiruta vyose, bivuye ku kibazo ca WikiLeaks. Uwaremye Bitcoin yashize ububasha bwo gukora uwo mugambi Martti Malmi na Gavin Andresen, abo bagabo babiri bamufashije mu bikorwa vyiwe vyo guteza imbere no gutanga amakuru.


Ivyo vyamushikiye inyuma y’aho ntibiramenyekana. Ubutumwa bukeyi bwasohotse mu nkuru ziwe zitandukanye ([Ishirahamwe P2P] [Vistomail](https://lists.linuxfoundation.org/pipermail/Bitcoin-dev/2015-My/010238.html)), ariko izo konti zishobora kuba zari zaciwe n’abantu. Ni co gituma akaranga ka Satoshi Nakamoto kaguma katazwi, kuko yashoboye kuguma atamenyekana biciye ku bikorwa vya Tor no ku bikorwa vyubahiriza ubuzima bwite.


Mu myaka iheze, haratanzwe ibimenyetso vyerekeye we, kandi amazina y’abantu bazwi cane nka Nick Szabo, Hal Finney, Adam Back canke Len Sassaman yaravuzwe. Mu mwaka w’2014, mbere vyemewe ko yari yabonetse mu muntu yitwa Dorian Prentice Satoshi Nakamoto, umuhinga mu vy’itumanaho, yari umunyamerika afise ubwenegihugu bw’igihugu, akomoka mu Buyapani, akaba na nyina wiwe mu gisagara ca Temple mu gisagara ca Los Angeles. Ariko rero, Satoshi iguma ari [akabanga](0ETcLj5jBy4).


Ivyo bihimba vy’akabanga bikikuje umuremyi wa Bitcoin vyavuzwe neza mu ncamake na Hal Finney muri Ruheshi 2013, uno akaba, muri [ubutumwa bwiwe bwa nyuma]. amajambo yo muri filime *Man of Steel* iherutse gusohoka:


> "Umuronka gute umuntu yamaze ubuzima bwiwe bwose atwikira imirongo yiwe?
>

> Ku bamwebamwe, yari umumarayika abarinda. Ku bandi, \[inkuru y’uruyeri,\] umuzimu, yama ari ukuntu itandukanye.
>

> S ihagarariye iki?"


## Umuryango uriko urafata ubutegetsi

<chapterId>16c5e6d6-2412-48c6-9687-6af92cf0d89a</chapterId>


Satoshi Nakamoto amaze kugenda, vyaciye biba ngombwa ko bagenda ata we bari kumwe. Igishimishije ni uko Bitcoin yari umugambi wuguruye umuntu wese yoshobora gutanga umusanzu, rero ukuzimangana kw’uwawushinze ntikwari ugupfa. Nk’uko umuhinguzi Jeff Garzik yavyanditse muri Nyakanga 2010 (ku bijanye n’uko uwushinze iyo nkuru yoba atahari):


> "Abantu barahagarika umutima cane ku vyerekeye amategeko n'ugushinga amategeko. Ariko ntaco bikenewe kugira ngo habeho umugambi wa Leta wo kubandanya, hano. Igihe cose kode y'inkomoko iguma yuguruye, ivyo birahagije. Niba hariho ivya nkenerwa, n'inyungu zihagije, abarundi bazobitanga. Nimwizere abarundi."

Ariko rero, ukwo kuzimangana ntikwari ata ngorane. Kuba ata Satoshi yariho vyasobanura ko ata bubasha bwari bukiriho uburongozi bwoshobora kuvako. Guhuza ibikorwa vyari bikenewe bivuye ku bijanye n’ugutegura porogarama be n’uguhanahana amakuru n’abandi. Abagize umuryango w’aba Bitcoin bariko barakura rero bategerezwa gukora utwigoro twinshi kugira ngo iyo migenzo ibe imwe.


### Iterambere ry'abanyagihugu


Nk’uko twabivuze, Gavin Andresen niwe yatwaye umugambi mu kwezi kwa kigarama 2010 mu guhingura ububiko bwa GitHub. Ku wa 13 Mukakaro 2011, yasavye imfashanyo ku nama mu gukora urudodo rwitwa "Imfashanyo y'iterambere rya Core Bitcoin Irakenewe". Mu mezi yakurikiye, abahinga mu bijanye n’amaporogarama benshi barakina maze batangura gutorera umuti ingorane. Muri abo harimwo Jeff Garzik, Pieter Wuille (sipa) na Wladimir van Der Laan (wumpus, laanwj). Abahinguzi bashasha nka Luka-Jr canke Matt Corallo (BlueMatt) na bo nyene bari muri ivyo. Abandi bantu barafashije ataco bashizeko mu buryo butaziguye kuri porogarama nyamukuru, nka Mike Hearn (yari muri iyo porogarama kuva mu kwezi kwa kigarama), yamenyesheje abantu bose ubuhinga bushasha bwo gushirwa mu ngiro bwitwa BitCoinJ muri Ntwarante 2011, kugira ngo hashirwe mu ngiro ubuhinga bwo kugenzura amahera yoroshe (SPV) nk’uko bivugwa mu gitabu cera.


Umugambi rusangi ni ugutuma uwo mugambi utera imbere mu buryo buramba. Ivyo birimwo gushinga uburenganzira bumwebumwe n’abantu benshi. Ku wa 19 Rusama, Mike Hearn [yasavye] ko abo bari muri uwo mugambi bakoresha izina ryabo ry'abanyagihugu, risobanura ko ari "abantu nyabo. Gavin, Mike n’abandi barahindura izina ryabo ry’uruyeri ku rubuga kugira ngo bagaragaze izina ryabo ryose. Urutonde rw’abahinguzi bakuru na rwo nyene [rwasohowe](https://web.archive.org/web/20110530221415/http://www.Bitcoin.org:80/) kuri paji ya mbere y’urubuga. Mu mpera z’ukwezi kwa Gitugutu, abahinguzi b’ivyo biganiro bashikirijwe nk’uko biri ni Gavin Andresen, Martti Malmi, Amir Taaki, Pieter Wuille, Nils Schneider na Jeff Garzik.


Guhuza ibikorwa na vyo nyene biratera imbere. Uretse ihuriro n'umurongo wa IRC #Bitcoin-dev, urutonde rw'abarungika ubutumwa rwerekeye iterambere rwitwa "Bitcoin-development" ruraboneka. Ni [ivyashizweho] ku wa 12 Ruheshi na Jeff Garzik. Bituma habaho ibiganiro ku buryo butegekanijwe ku mahinduka azokorwa kuri Bitcoin. Ibiganiro ku bijanye n’[ikarata y’inzira] y’uwo mugambi biratangura mu kwezi kwa munani. Urutonde rwa mbere rwashizwe kuri SourceForge; izokwimurirwa ku rubuga rwa Linux Foundation muri Ruheshi 2015, imbere y’uko amaherezo [yimurirwa] ku rubuga rwa Linux Foundation muri Ruheshi 2015. Amatsinda mu ntango z'umwaka w'2024.


Ku wa 19 Nzero 2011, Amir Taaki [yatanguje] uburyo bw’Ivyiyumviro vy’Iterambere vy’Igihugu ca Bitcoin (Ivyiyumviro vy’Iterambere ry’Igihugu ca Bitcoin), bishingiye ku citegererezo ca P ururimi rwo gukora porogarama. Izo BIPs ni inyandiko zidondora ivyoshobora guhindurwa mu masezerano canke zitanga amakuru rusangi ku kibano. Adondora ingene ivyo bigenda biciye ku BIP-1, iyo BIP-2 ya Luke-Jr izosubirira mu nyuma. Ivyo vyiyumviro bitangura kwakirwa kuri [wiki ya Bitcoin](wiki.


Mu burongozi bwa Gavin Andresen, harasohotse amaverisiyo menshi y’iyo porogarama mu mezi: [v0.3.20] (https. [v0.3.21] (insanganyamatsiko=6642.msg97074#msg97074) ku wa 27 Ndamukiza, [v0.3.22](intangamarara 5, [v0.3.23](igenekerezo rya 13 Ruheshi, n’igenekerezo rya 13 Ruheshi, n’i [v0.3.24](v0.3.24](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=27187.msg342270#msg342270) ku wa 8 Nyakanga. Ku wa 23 Nzero 2011, verisiyo nshasha nini, verisiyo 0.4, yarasohotse ku mugaragaro . [yasohotse](yasohotse](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=45410.msg541446#msg541446), mu buryo bw’ikigereranyo vyerekana ko ugukurikirana kw’iterambere kwariko kuragenda neza.


### Urubuga, Ihuriro, na Wiki


Gutegura porogarama si co kintu conyene gikeneye gucungirwa iyo Satoshi itahari. Hariho kandi ibikoresho rusangi vyo guhanahana amakuru nk'urubuga, ihuriro, na wiki. Ivyo ni vyo vy'ukuri "amadirisho y'amaduka" y'uwo mugambi, kandi ingene bicungirwa birahambaye cane.


Nk’uko twabibonye, ​​amaze kugenda, Satoshi yarahaye ububasha bwo kugenzura urubuga Martti Malmi, uwo muhora rero ukaba urimwo ihuriro (Bitcoin.org/smf) n’urubuga [wiki](20110102000201/http. (Bitcoin/wiki). Ariko rero, Martti yari afise umwanya muto wo kwihebera ico gikorwa. Kuva mu mpera z’umwaka w’2010, yari [afise vyinshi akora] n’akazi ko kwimenyereza, hanyuma akora akazi k’igihe cose, buhoro buhoro asubira inyuma.


Kubera ukubura umwanya, Martti yaciye ategekwa gufunga buhoro buhoro urubuga rwiwe rwa Exchange, BitcoinExchange. Yari ivuye ku murongo mu gihe c’ihinduka ry’umurongo mu kwezi kwa kigarama 2010. Mu kwezi kwa mbere, [yafashe ingingo] yo kutayikoresha. Mu ntango z’ukwezi kwa Myandagaro, [yagurishije] izina ry’urubuga ku mahera 250 y’ama bitcoins, angana n’amadolari 2.365 ico gihe. Iryo huriro ryoca risubira ku musozi Gox.


Ariko mbere na mbere ni uburongozi bw’urubuga Martti akeneye guha abandi. Mu mpera z’umwaka w’2010 no mu ntango z’umwaka w’2011, Bitcoin.org yarahuye n’abantu bamwebamwe. [ibibazo] (ivy'ubuhinga bwa none). Ku wa 28 Ntwarante, Martti [yashizeho] itangazo ku rubuga asaba imfashanyo y’ubuhinga kandi aronka inyishu nyinshi. Ivyo bikaba vyatumye urubuga rudashobora gusohoka ku rubuga n’abashitsi benshi cane.


Ivyo vyasa na vyo nyene vyarahindutse. Mu kwezi kwa kigarama 2010, urubuga rwari rukiri nk’urwo mu gihe ca Satoshi. Aha niho hari [ifoto] (urubuga.ububiko.org/urubuga/20101110005546/www.Bitcoin.org/) kuva ku wa 5 Kigarama:


![Snapshot of Bitcoin.org from December 5, 2010](assets/en/061.webp)


Gutyo, ibara ryongereweko mu ntango z’umwaka w’2011:


![Snapshot of Bitcoin.org from February 16, 2011](assets/en/062.webp)


Muri Ndamukiza, urubuga rwahindutse kubera ugusubira guhingura [kwatunganijwe](https://bitcointalk.org/index.php?topic=4223.msg80581#msg80581) n’abanyagihugu. Ehe uko [vyasa] (urubuga.ububiko.org/urubuga/20110411071904/) hanyuma:


![Snapshot of Bitcoin.org from April 11, 2011](assets/en/063.webp)


Ubwa nyuma, muri Nzero 2011, hariho ihinduka rishasha [rakozwe] na Nils Schneider. Ububiko bushasha bwa GitHub bwararemwe ku bw’ico kintu. Iyi nzira yomara igihe kirekire: ntiyohindurwa gushika mu 2013. Ng'iyi (menya ko Bitcoin-the-software rero idondorwa nk'"umugambi w'inkomoko yuguruye utwawe n'abanyagihugu"):


![Snapshot of Bitcoin.org from September 23, 2011](assets/en/064.webp)


Ku bijanye na wiki, mu ntango yari ishingiye kuri DokuWiki, moteri y’ubuntu yinjijwe mu rubuga. Ariko rero, mu kwezi kwa kigarama 2010, Mark Karpelès, umuhinga mu vy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga bw’ivy’ubuhinga. Iyi wiki ishingiye kuri moteri ya MediaWiki, iyo abona ko ari nziza cane kandi yoroshe gukoresha. Iciyumviro ca mbere si ugusubirira inyandiko zisanzweho, ariko, nk'uko Mark abivuga, gutegura "wiki idasanzwe, ishingiye ku kibano."


Iyi wiki nshasha irasaba [Martti Malmi] (Iciyumviro=2321.msg30873#msg30873) na [Gavin Andresen](Iciyumviro=2321.msg30873), quick351msg3 bikaba biyigira wiki nyamukuru. Aha niho [ifoto](ifoto] yafashwe ku wa 21 Rusama:


![Snapshot of the Bitcoin.it wiki on May 21, 2011](assets/en/065.webp)


Haciye imisi mikeyi itangujwe, urubuga rwitwa "wiki" ruri kuri paji y'intango ya Bitcoin.org [ibiharuro]. Ibirimwo biragenda biva muri verisiyo ya DokuWiki. Ku wa 31 Mukakaro, Martti [yerekanye] ku rubuga rw’ihuriro ko iyi ari wiki nshasha.


Ica gatatu ni ihuriro rya Bitcoin. Martti ni we arayirongora, ariko aca yihuta gutora abayirongora. Umwe muri bo ni Theymos (izina ryiwe ry’ukuri Michael Marquardt), aronka amabanga y’inyongera, cane cane gufasha mu gucunga iyo nama. Iryo huriro rikorera kuri moteri y’ihuriro ry’amamashini yoroshe kandi ntiryahinduye uko rigaragara mu myaka iheze. Ariko rero, URL yayo yarahindutse incuro zibiri. Ubwa mbere, ku wa 17 Rusama, ihuriro [rimuriwe] ku ihuriro.Bitcoin.org. Hanyuma, ku wa 1 Myandagaro, [rijanwa] mu kibanza gishasha co ku rwego rwo hejuru: bitcointalk.org. Mu myaka izoza, izokwitwa BitcoinTalk.

Kubera ko agaciro k’amahera kariyongereye mu ci c’umwaka w’2011, Martti Malmi [yagurishije] igice kinini c’amahera yiwe y’ubuhinga bwa none kugira ngo yigurire inzu nziza hafi y’igisagara ca Helsinki. Hanyuma, [arasiga] akazi kiwe kugira ngo amare amezi makeyi mu Buyapani. Yahevye urubuga n’ihuriro, [aragenda] [bo] (bo] mu minwe ya Theymos n’umuntu umwe yitwa Cøbra, [vyasobanuwe](https://forum.Bitcoin.com/ama-mbaze-ikintu cose/ndi-m-martti-malmi-mbere-ya-Bitcoin-kandi-uwashinze-w'intango-amahuriro-y'ama-bitcointalk-org-ama-t2770.h Satoshi." Abo bagabo babiri borongoye hamwe izo nzira zompi mu myaka yakurikiye.


### Inama n'amakoraniro


Ugusohoka kw’uwashinze n’ugukenera gukorana ntibigira ico bikoze ku ruhande rw’ubuhinga gusa ariko kandi biragira ico bikoze ku ruhande rw’imibano, ivyo bikaba bifasha gukomeza umuryango mu gutuma habaho amasano hagati y’abanywanyi. Ni co gituma amateraniro n'inama bitegurwa "mu buzima nyakuri." Ivyo birori kandi birafise akamaro ko kumenyekanisha Bitcoin ku bantu bashobora guhangana n’ibintu biri kuri Internet.


Amakoraniro ya mbere y'abakoresha Bitcoin yatangujwe na Bruce Wagner, umunyamakuru w'ikinyamakuru [YouTube](https://www.youtube.com/@vlogwrap) co muri New York kirimwo impaka za televiziyo ku bijanye n'ubuhinga, aho yashinze ikiganiro citwa **Bitcoin ca mbere mu kwezi kwa Ndamukiza cane.** i New York kw'igenekerezo rya 11 Kigarama 2010 (UTC). Hanyuma, inama y'ubwo bwoko nyene **yabaye** i Washington D.C. **vyateguwe** ku wa 5 Ruhuhuma 2011, i Zurich mu Busuwisi na Mike Hearn, hamwe na Christian Decker na Stefan Thomas (justmoon) bari kumwe na bo.

Ukwezi kwa kabiri kandi ni kwo kwerekana [ikiganiro ca mbere cafashwe amasanamu] (Ikiganiro ca Bitcoin), carongowe na Gavin Andresen ku wa 8 mu gihe c’umusi mukuru wateguwe mu gisagara ciwe c’amavukiro ca Amherst, muri Massachusetts. Ivyo biganiro vyiswe n’umuyobozi mushasha w’uwo mugambi birimwo indimi nyinshi Elements zoshobora kugaragaza uburyo amafaranga y’amahera azoshikirizwa mu myaka ikurikira.


:::id ya videwo = 92b9aa30-1479-4d4f-b57f-f07b660145f2::


Naho ibintu vya mbere vyabaye muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika, umuryango w’Abafaransa ntiwasigaye inyuma. Ku wa 25 Rusama, kugira ngo Gavin Andresen agendere i Paris, mu karere ka La Défense harateguwe ifunguro ry’umutaga, ryitabiriwe n’abantu bazwi cane nka Lucien Grondin, David François na Jon Matonis (na we nyene yariko aragendera).


![Meeting at La Défense in Paris with Gavin Andresen, in a pink shirt](assets/en/066.webp)

Inama ya La Défense i Paris na Gavin Andresen, yambaye ishati y’ibara ry’agahama (inkomoko: [ububiko bw’ihuriro]


Haciye ukwezi kumwe, ku wa 15 Ruheshi, igikorwa ca mbere co gushikiriza abantu bose igitabu Bitcoin mu gifaransa [carabaye], na co nyene i Paris. Yarongowe na Renaud Lifchitz (nono2357), umuhinga mu vy’umutekano wo kuri internet akiri muto yari yaravumbuye Bitcoin umwaka umwe imbere y’aho. Ivyo [vyashikirijwe] vyari vyiza cane, kandi abantu bari baje bari beza cane ku buryo icumba cari cuzuye.


![Bitcoin presentation by Renaud Lifchitz on June 15, 2011](assets/en/067.webp)

Bitcoin yashikirijwe na Renaud Lifchitz ku wa 15 Ruheshi 2011 (isoko: [ububiko bw'ihuriro]


Kubera ivyo bintu vyabaye, umuryango w’i Paris [warateguye] ikoraniro ry’abantu ku wa 11 Nyakanga, ico gikorwa carahuje abantu nka Pierre Noizat na Émilien Dutang.

Ku ruhande mpuzamakungu, inama ya mbere y’abantu bose ku bijanye na Bitcoin yabaye kuva kw’igenekerezo rya 19 gushika ku rya 21 Myandagaro i New York.
